If you are using an AI prototyping tool such as [Lovable](https://lovable.dev?utm_source=chatgpt.com), [Bolt.new](https://bolt.new?utm_source=chatgpt.com), [v0 by Vercel](https://v0.dev?utm_source=chatgpt.com), or [Figma AI](https://www.figma.com/ai/?utm_source=chatgpt.com), use the prompt below.

# Connect AI – Complete Product Prototype Prompt

Design a modern enterprise SaaS platform called **Connect AI**, an AI-powered Recruitment, Assessment, and Talent Intelligence Platform for organizations in Saudi Arabia and the GCC.

The platform should support both Arabic (RTL) and English (LTR) and be designed with enterprise-grade UX similar to Workday, Greenhouse, Lever, and Elevatus.

## Product Vision

Connect AI helps organizations automate and optimize the entire recruitment lifecycle from job creation to onboarding through AI-powered screening, matching, assessments, video interviews, analytics, and talent intelligence.

The platform serves:

* HR Teams
* Recruiters
* Hiring Managers
* Department Heads
* Candidates
* External Interviewers
* System Administrators

---

# Main Modules

## 1. Executive Dashboard

Display:

* Total Open Jobs
* Applications Received
* Candidates in Pipeline
* Time to Hire
* Cost per Hire
* Offer Acceptance Rate
* Source of Hire
* AI Matching Accuracy
* Candidate Drop-off Rate
* Diversity Metrics
* Recruitment Funnel

Widgets:

* Hiring Pipeline
* Upcoming Interviews
* Jobs Needing Attention
* AI Recommendations
* Recruitment Performance Trends

---

## 2. Job Management

Features:

* Create Job
* AI Generate Job Description
* AI Generate Responsibilities
* AI Generate Skills
* AI Generate Interview Questions
* AI Generate Assessment Questions

Fields:

* Job Title
* Department
* Location
* Employment Type
* Grade
* Salary Range
* Skills
* Requirements
* Hiring Manager
* Number of Openings

Views:

* List View
* Kanban View
* Analytics View

---

## 3. Career Portal

Candidate-facing portal.

Features:

* Search Jobs
* Apply Online
* Candidate Registration
* Social Login
* CV Upload
* LinkedIn Import
* Profile Builder

Candidate Dashboard:

* Applied Jobs
* Assessment Status
* Interview Status
* Offers
* Notifications

---

## 4. AI CV Parsing

Upload CV and automatically extract:

* Name
* Email
* Phone
* Education
* Certifications
* Experience
* Skills
* Languages
* Projects

Display:

* Parsed CV View
* Candidate Summary
* AI Recommendations

---

## 5. AI Candidate Matching Engine

Automatically match candidates against jobs.

Scoring Factors:

* Skills Match
* Experience Match
* Education Match
* Industry Match
* Certifications
* Language Proficiency

Output:

* Match Percentage
* Strength Areas
* Missing Skills
* Hiring Recommendation

---

## 6. Applicant Tracking System (ATS)

Pipeline Stages:

1. Applied
2. Screening
3. Assessment
4. AI Interview
5. HR Interview
6. Technical Interview
7. Hiring Manager Interview
8. Offer
9. Hired
10. Rejected

Features:

* Drag and Drop Kanban
* Bulk Actions
* Notes
* Tags
* Candidate History
* Internal Comments

---

## 7. AI Assessment Platform

Assessment Types:

* Multiple Choice
* Technical Questions
* Coding Tests
* Written Responses
* Psychometric Tests
* Custom Assessments

AI Features:

* Generate Assessments
* Auto Evaluation
* Score Analysis
* Benchmarking

Dashboard:

* Assessment Results
* Candidate Ranking
* Pass/Fail Recommendation

---

## 8. AI Video Interviewing

One-way video interviews.

Workflow:

Candidate enters interview portal.

System displays question.

Candidate records answer.

AI analyzes:

* Transcript
* Communication Skills
* Confidence
* Language Quality
* Response Relevance
* Sentiment
* Engagement

Arabic and English supported.

Output:

* AI Score
* Competency Score
* Hiring Recommendation
* Video Recording
* Transcript

---

## 9. AI Recruiter Assistant

ChatGPT-style assistant.

Capabilities:

* Search Candidates
* Generate Job Descriptions
* Create Assessments
* Suggest Interview Questions
* Generate Hiring Reports
* Candidate Insights
* Recruitment Recommendations

Natural language search:

"Show me senior product managers with fintech experience."

<attached-skill name="Design System (design system)">
[Design System] This project uses the **Design System** design system. This is a binding choice for visual style — every visual must follow it. Don't invent colors, type, spacing, or components not grounded here.

Scope: the design system is a visual style reference only. Its guide may describe example products, brands, or people that are unrelated to the user and unrelated to the subject of this conversation. Never treat anything in the design system as a fact about the user, their work, or the topic they asked about.

    Explore it to find what you need:
    - Always copy out the fonts and colors you need
    - For prototypes and designs, always copy out any relevant components
    - If the design system contains existing mocks of products, and you were asked to design or prototype something similar, copy and fork those mocks to start your design. This helps you make high-quality designs.

    Explore it quickly to find relevant UI kits (e.g. mocks of existing products you can copy and fork)

Full system at `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`. Before producing any visuals, explore it: call `list_files("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/")` to see the structure, then `read_file` the README/base.md or whatever index file it has. Don't guess at the design system's contents.

CSS tokens: the guide may describe tokens in prose, but the exact `--*` names are defined in the design system's stylesheet(s). Before writing any `var(--*)`, look up the real name in the design system's `.css` files (`list_files` + `read_file` under `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`). Never guess a token name — an unresolved `var()` silently falls back to the browser default.

For assets and UI kits beyond the guide: `read_file("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/<path>")` and `copy_files` to bring them into the current project.

**Connect AI** is ready — a high-fidelity, bilingual (EN/AR + RTL) recruiting platform prototype covering the full recruiter flow.

**What's built (all clickable, real state):**
- **Executive Dashboard** — KPIs, recruitment funnel with conversion rates, performance trends, AI recommendations, upcoming interviews, source-of-hire, Saudization
- **Job Management** — list/board/analytics views + a 4-step **Create Job wizard with live AI generation** (description streams in, skills & interview questions auto-populate)
- **ATS Pipeline** — 8-stage **drag-and-drop Kanban**, AI-ranked, filterable by job
- **Candidate 360** — AI summary, match breakdown, parsed CV, experience timeline, feedback, activity, with advance/reject actions that flow back to the pipeline
- **AI Assessment** — candidate ranking leaderboard, benchmark comparison, section scores, recommendation
- **AI Video Interview** — playable mock player, transcript with AI-flagged keywords, competency analysis, sentiment
- **Offer Management** — approval workflow, generated offer letter, GCC salary breakdown

**System:** IBM Plex Sans / Plex Sans Arabic / Plex Mono, refined indigo + teal "AI" accent, full light/dark themes. **Tweaks panel** (and topbar) controls language, theme, accent, and comfortable/compact density — all persisted.

**Notes & next steps:**
- Scoped to the recruiter slice you chose; the other modules (Career Portal, CV parsing module, Talent CRM, Integrations, White-label, etc.) aren't in this build — happy to add any next.
- Realistic Saudi/GCC sample data throughout; the video player and AI generation are simulated front-end behaviors.

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (201 lines)">
Design a Permissions & Access Control feature for "Connect AI", an existing 
AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This is a NEW feature added to a LIVE 
product — match the established visual language exactly. Do not redesign 
the existing UI.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow (no heavy elevation)
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (e.g., "MAIN", "HIRING").
  Active items have a light lavender background, deep purple text (#6B5BFF), 
  and a thin purple left-border indicator. Count badges right-aligned in gray.
- TOP BAR: search input with "AI" teal badge inside it, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell, primary "+ Create" button in solid 
  purple (#6B5BFF)
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF range)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4 range) used only for AI-related badges 
  on light teal backgrounds
- Typography: clean sans-serif, large bold numbers for metrics
- Soft pastel pill badges with deeper text (e.g., teal bg + teal text)
- Segmented controls: white pill on light gray track
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke, minimal
- Logo: "Connect AI" wordmark + small purple sparkle in a dark rounded square
- Sidebar bottom: circular avatar with initial, user name, role title, 
  with a "Collapse" affordance above it
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render this design in English

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SIDEBAR — ADD A NEW SECTION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Below the existing "HIRING" section (Jobs, Pipeline, Assessments, Video 
Interviews, Offers), add a new section header "ADMIN" with these items:
- Users  (count badge: 47)
- Roles
- Workflows
- Email Templates

Render "Users" as the active item.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WHAT TO BUILD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
A single self-contained React artifact with THREE views the user navigates 
between via state. Use lucide-react for icons. Use useState for view 
switching and all interactivity.

─────────────────────────────────────────
VIEW 1 — USERS LIST  (default)
─────────────────────────────────────────
Page header:
  Title "Users"
  Subtitle "Manage who can access Connect AI and what they can do."
  Right side: "Invite user" primary purple button

Stat row (4 small cards, dashboard-style but compact, no trend lines):
  Total users 47   |   Active 42   |   Pending invites 3   |   Suspended 2

Filter bar:
  Search input, "All roles" dropdown, "All statuses" dropdown

Users table with columns:
  - User (avatar circle with initials + name + email under)
  - Role (pastel pill badge — Admin: purple, Recruiter: blue, 
    Hiring Manager: orange, Interviewer: teal, Custom: gray)
  - Jobs (number, e.g. "5 jobs", clickable look)
  - Status (colored dot + label: Active green, Pending amber, Suspended gray)
  - Last active (relative time, e.g. "2h ago")
  - Actions (three-dot kebab menu)

Populate with 9 realistic users, mixing Arabic and English names:
  Layla Al-Fayez (Admin, Active), Ahmed Hassan (Recruiter, Active), 
  Sara Mansour (Recruiter, Active), Khalid Al-Rahman (Hiring Manager, Active), 
  Fatima Al-Shamsi (Hiring Manager, Active), Omar Saleh (Hiring Manager, Pending), 
  Noura Al-Otaibi (Interviewer, Active), James Mitchell (Interviewer, Active),
  Priya Sharma (Custom — "External Reviewer", Suspended)

Clicking a row navigates to View 2 for that user.

─────────────────────────────────────────
VIEW 2 — USER DETAIL & PERMISSIONS
─────────────────────────────────────────
Breadcrumb: "Users › Ahmed Hassan"
Header card:
  Large avatar, name, email, role badge, status dot
  Right side: "Edit user" secondary button, "Suspend" ghost button

Two-column layout:

LEFT COLUMN (60%):
  Card "Role & Permissions"
    - Current role dropdown (e.g. Recruiter) with "Manage roles" link
    - Sub-label "Permission overrides for this user (2)"
    - Shows any individual grants/revocations on top of the role
  
  Card "Permissions by category"
    - Expandable accordion sections, each showing 
      "X of Y permissions granted" summary on the right
    - Categories listed below — render "Candidates" expanded by default 
      to demonstrate the toggle UI:
    
    ▸ Jobs
        jobs.view, jobs.create, jobs.edit, jobs.archive, jobs.manage_team
    ▾ Candidates  (EXPANDED)
        candidates.view  — with sub-dropdown when ON:
            ○ All candidates  ● Candidates on jobs I'm assigned to  ○ Only my assigned candidates
        candidates.move
        candidates.edit
        candidates.delete
        candidates.self_assign_interview
    ▸ Interviews
        interviews.schedule, interviews.conduct, 
        interviews.scorecard_submit, interviews.scorecard_view_others
    ▸ Workflows
        workflows.view, workflows.create, workflows.edit
    ▸ Email Templates
        templates.view, templates.create, templates.edit, templates.send_manual
    ▸ Offers
        offers.create, offers.approve, offers.send
    ▸ Settings
        settings.manage_users, settings.manage_roles, 
        settings.manage_integrations, settings.audit_log
    
    Each permission is a row with: name, short description, toggle switch.
    Show ONE soft amber warning bar inline somewhere: 
      "Heads up: 'Submit scorecard' is on but 'Conduct interviews' is off — 
       this user can score interviews they didn't conduct."

RIGHT COLUMN (40%):
  Card "Jobs this user is on" (4 rows)
    Each row: job title, department, access level pill 
    (Browse only / Interview / Full access)
    e.g. "Senior Frontend Engineer · Engineering · Full access"
  
  Card "Recent activity" (last 5 actions, plain list with time-ago)
    e.g. "Moved Sara Mansour to Interview · 2h ago"
         "Submitted scorecard for Khalid Al-Rahman · yesterday"

─────────────────────────────────────────
VIEW 3 — ROLES MANAGEMENT
─────────────────────────────────────────
Reached via sidebar "Roles" item or "Manage roles" link in View 2.

Page header:
  Title "Roles"
  Subtitle "Define what each role can do across the platform."
  Right side: "+ Create custom role" primary purple button

Grid of role cards (2 columns on desktop):
  
  System roles (badge "System" in small gray pill, cannot delete):
    1. Admin       — purple badge, "Full access to everything" — 1 member, 
                     "23 of 23 permissions"
    2. Recruiter   — blue badge, "Manage candidates, jobs, and outreach" — 
                     2 members, "16 of 23 permissions"
    3. Hiring Manager — orange badge, "Make hiring decisions on assigned jobs" —

[Design System] This project uses the **Design System** design system. This is a binding choice for visual style — every visual must follow it. Don't invent colors, type, spacing, or components not grounded here.

Scope: the design system is a visual style reference only. Its guide may describe example products, brands, or people that are unrelated to the user and unrelated to the subject of this conversation. Never treat anything in the design system as a fact about the user, their work, or the topic they asked about.

    Explore it to find what you need:
    - Always copy out the fonts and colors you need
    - For prototypes and designs, always copy out any relevant components
    - If the design system contains existing mocks of products, and you were asked to design or prototype something similar, copy and fork those mocks to start your design. This helps you make high-quality designs.

    Explore it quickly to find relevant UI kits (e.g. mocks of existing products you can copy and fork)

Full system at `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`. Before producing any visuals, explore it: call `list_files("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/")` to see the structure, then `read_file` the README/base.md or whatever index file it has. Don't guess at the design system's contents.

CSS tokens: the guide may describe tokens in prose, but the exact `--*` names are defined in the design system's stylesheet(s). Before writing any `var(--*)`, look up the real name in the design system's `.css` files (`list_files` + `read_file` under `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`). Never guess a token name — an unresolved `var()` silently falls back to the browser default.

For assets and UI kits beyond the guide: `read_file("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/<path>")` and `copy_files` to bring them into the current project.

    - On hover: subtle scale-up + shadow lift + "Configure" hint

    - A subtle horizontal connector line in light gray
    - A small "+" button at the midpoint, visible on hover only, that says 
      "Insert stage" on tooltip

  After the last main-flow stage (Offer) before the terminals:
    - A persistent "+ Add stage" dashed-border placeholder card

  - Stage name (text input)

  - Required toggle: "Required stage" / "Optional — can be skipped"
  - Color accent (5 small color swatches: gray, blue, purple, teal, amber)

  - Toggle at top: "Send an email when candidates enter this stage" 
    (ON for this example)

    - Email template picker (showing "Screening Call Invitation" selected,

        ☑ Candidate
        ☐ Hiring manager
        ☐ Recruiter

        ☐ Custom user… (with picker)

        ● Auto-send immediately

      "After 1 business day" / "Custom…"

    entry to this stage" with a "+ Set up email" link

──── MOVEMENT RULES TAB ────
  - "Who can move candidates into this stage" — chip multi-select:
    [Admin] [Recruiter] [Hiring Manager] [Interviewer]   (HM and Recruiter 
    selected by default)
  - "Required before moving forward" — checkboxes:
    ☐ All assigned interviewers have submitted scorecards
    ☐ Assessment is completed
    ☐ Hiring manager approval recorded
    ☑ Rejection reason captured  (visible only on terminal Rejected stage)
  - "Stage SLA" — optional field: "Notify if candidate sits here longer 
    than [3] business days" with a "+ Add escalation" link below

Panel footer (sticky bottom):
  - "Remove stage" ghost button (red text)
    — clicking shows a small inline warning: "3 candidates are currently 
    in this stage. Move them before removing."
  - "Done" primary button (closes the panel; changes already auto-saved)

Design an Email Templates feature for "Connect AI", an existing AI-powered 
HR recruitment platform. This is a NEW feature added to a LIVE product — 
match the established visual language exactly. Do not redesign the existing UI.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items have a light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), and a thin purple left-border indicator. Count badges 
  right-aligned in gray.
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, dark-mode 
  toggle, notification bell, primary "+ Create" button in solid purple
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF range)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4 range) for AI-related badges on 
  light teal backgrounds
- Typography: clean sans-serif, large bold numbers for metrics
- Soft pastel pill badges with deeper text
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke, minimal (use lucide-react)
- Logo: "Connect AI" + small purple sparkle in dark rounded square
- Sidebar bottom: circular avatar with initial, user name, role title
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English for this design

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SIDEBAR NAVIGATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN
  - Dashboard
HIRING
  - Jobs (8)
  - Pipeline (64)
  - Assessments
  - Video Interviews
  - Offers (5)
ADMIN
  - Users (47)
  - Roles
  - Workflows
  - Email Templates  ← ACTIVE

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WHAT TO BUILD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
A single self-contained React artifact with THREE views the user navigates 
between via state. Use lucide-react for icons. Use useState for view 
switching and interactivity.

─────────────────────────────────────────
VIEW 1 — TEMPLATES LIBRARY  (default)
─────────────────────────────────────────
Page header:
  Title "Email Templates"
  Subtitle "Manage automated and ad-hoc emails sent to candidates and 
  your team."
  Right side: "Manage variables" ghost button + "+ New template" primary 
  purple button

Stat row (4 small cards, dashboard-style but compact, no trend lines):
  Total templates 18  |  Active 16  |  Linked to workflows 12  |  
  Languages used 2

Filter bar:
  Search input, "All categories ▾", "All languages ▾", "All statuses ▾"

Section heading: "Starter templates" with subtitle 
  "Pre-written templates by Connect AI. Use them as-is or customize."

Grid of starter template cards (3 columns):
  1. Application Received — Application — EN — used in 4 workflows
  2. Recruiter Screen Invitation — Screening — EN — used in 3 workflows
  3. Interview Invitation — Interview — EN — used in 5 workflows
  4. Interview Reminder — Interview — EN — used in 2 workflows
  5. Assessment Invitation — Assessment — EN — used in 3 workflows
  6. Rejection — Pre-Interview — Rejection — EN — used in 2 workflows
  7. Rejection — Post-Interview — Rejection — EN — used in 3 workflows
  8. Offer Extension — Offer — EN — used in 4 workflows
  9. Welcome / Hired — Onboarding — EN — used in 4 workflows

Section heading: "Your templates" with right-aligned filter

Grid of custom template cards (3 columns):
  - Senior Engineer Technical Brief — Interview — EN — 1 workflow
  - دعوة لمقابلة فنية (Technical Interview Invite) — Interview — AR — 2 workflows
  - Executive Offer (Confidential) — Offer — EN — 1 workflow
  - Internal Transfer Notice — Internal — EN — 1 workflow
  - Sales Final Round Confirmation — Interview — EN — 0 workflows (draft state)
  - + Create from scratch  (dashed-border card at the end)

Each template card shows:
  - Top: small category pill (color-coded — Application: blue, Screening: 
    teal, Interview: purple, Assessment: amber, Rejection: gray, Offer: 
    green, Onboarding: pink, Internal: indigo)
  - Template name (medium weight)
  - Subject line preview (one line, gray, truncated with "…")
  - Bottom row: language tag (EN/AR with small flag-style pill), 
    "Used in X workflows" link, three-dot kebab menu (Edit / Duplicate / 
    Send test / Archive)
  - Subtle border-left in the category color (2px)
  - Starter templates have a small "Starter" gray pill in top-right corner

Clicking any card opens VIEW 2 for that template.

─────────────────────────────────────────
VIEW 2 — TEMPLATE EDITOR  (main work surface)
─────────────────────────────────────────
Breadcrumb: "Email Templates › Interview Invitation"

Header strip:
  Left side:
    - Template name (inline-editable on click)
    - Row below: category pill + language pill (EN) + "Active" status pill 
      + "Used in 5 workflows" link (gray, clickable)
  Right side:
    - "Send test" ghost button (envelope icon)
    - "Duplicate" ghost icon button
    - Auto-save indicator: "All changes saved · just now" (gray text with 
      small checkmark)

Two-column main layout:

LEFT COLUMN (55% — EDITOR):

  Section "Email details" (white card):
    - From: dropdown ("careers@connect-ai.com" selected)
    - Reply-to: dropdown ("Use platform threading (default)" selected, 
      with helper text "Replies thread automatically to candidate profile.")
    - Default recipient(s): chip multi-select 
      [Candidate ✓]  with "+ Add recipient" — options: Hiring Manager, 
      Recruiter, Assigned Interviewer(s), Custom user
    - Helper note: "When linked to a workflow stage, recipients can be 
      overridden per stage."

  Section "Subject line" (white card):
    - Text input with character counter ("42 / 78") in the corner
    - Pre-filled: "Interview invitation for {{job.title}} at {{company.name}}"
    - Variables rendered as purple chips inline, not raw text
    - "+ Insert variable" button on the right opens variable picker

  Section "Body" (white card, the largest):
    - Rich text toolbar across the top: Bold, Italic, Underline, 
      Bullet list, Numbered list, Link, Blockquote, Heading dropdown, 
      "+ Insert variable", "+ Attach file"
    - Editor area with realistic email body content:
      
      "Hi {{candidate.first_name}},
      
      Thanks for your application for the {{job.title}} role on our 
      {{job.department}} team. We've reviewed your background and would 
      love to invite you to an interview.
      
      Your interview is scheduled with {{interviewer.name}} on 
      {{interview.date}} at {{interview.time}}.
      
      📎 Please use this link to join: {{interview.link}}
      
      If you need to reschedule, you can pick a new time here: 
      {{scheduling_link}}
      
      Looking forward to speaking with you.
      
      Best,
      {{recruiter.name}}
      {{company.name}} Talent Team"
    
    - Variables shown as purple inline chips (e.g., a small pill saying 
      "candidate.first_name" with purple bg and purple text, not the raw 
      "{{...}}" syntax)
    - Footer below editor: "✦ AI suggestions" link (teal accent) — 
      "Improve tone", "Translate to Arabic", "Suggest subject lines"

  Section "Attachments" (white card, collapsed by default):
    - "No attachments. + Add static file or dynamic attachment"

RIGHT COLUMN (45% — LIVE PREVIEW):

  Sticky preview pane (white card, taller):
  
  Top bar of the preview card:
    - "Preview as" dropdown: "Ahmed Hassan — Senior Frontend Engineer" 
      selected (with small avatar)
    - Toggle group on the right: [Desktop] [Mobile]
  
  Below the preview controls, render an email-client-style mockup:
    - Header row: "From: Connect AI Talent <careers@connect-ai.com>"
    - "To: ahmed.hassan@email.com"
    - "Subject: Interview invitation for Senior Frontend Engineer at Connect AI"
    - Divider
    - Rendered body with all variables resolved using Ahmed's data
    - Show realistic resolved values (interview date "Tuesday, June 11 
      at 2:00 PM GST", interviewer name "Khalid Al-Rahman", etc.)
    - Footer auto-appended: small gray text "Sent via Connect AI · 
      Unsubscribe" (only on non-transactional categories — here it shows 
      as transactional, so no unsubscribe)
  
  Below the preview:
    - "Unresolved variables: 0" with green checkmark
    - If any variable were unresolved, show "Unresolved variables: 2 — 
      {{custom.team_lead_name}}, {{custom.office_address}}" in soft amber 
      warning style

Bottom strip (full width, light gray separator above):
  Section "Used in workflows" (white card):
    - List of 5 workflow → stage references where this template is linked:
      • Standard Hire → Recruiter Screen
      • Engineering — Senior → Recruiter Screen
      • Engineering — Junior → Phone Screen
      • Sales — Account Executive → Discovery Call
      • Internship Program 2026 → Initial Chat
    - Each row clickable (would navigate to the workflow)
    - "+ Link to a workflow stage" link at the bottom

VARIABLE PICKER (appears when "+ Insert variable" is clicked):
  A small dropdown panel (~360px wide) with:
    - Search input at top: "Search variables…"
    - Tabs: "System" | "Custom"
    - Scrollable list grouped by source:
        Candidate
          candidate.first_name (text) — "Ahmed"
          candidate.last_name (text) — "Hassan"
          candidate.full_name (text) — "Ahmed Hassan"
          candidate.email (text) — "ahmed.hassan@email.com"
          candidate.phone (text)
        Job
          job.title — "Senior Frontend Engineer"
          job.department — "Engineering"
          job.location — "Riyadh, KSA"
        Interview
          interview.date, interview.time, interview.link, 
          interviewer.name
        Company
          company.name — "Connect AI"
        Recruiter
          recruiter.name, recruiter.email
        Scheduling
          scheduling_link
    - Each row hover-highlights, clicking inserts the variable chip at 
      cursor position
    - Bottom: "+ Create custom variable" link

─────────────────────────────────────────
VIEW 3 — VARIABLES MANAGEMENT
─────────────────────────────────────────
Reached from "Manage variables" in View 1 header or "+ Create custom 
variable" in the variable picker.

Page header:
  Title "Variables"
  Subtitle "Personalize emails with data from candidates, jobs, and your 
  custom fields."
  Right side: "+ New custom variable" primary purple button

Tab navigation (underline style):
  [System variables] [Custom variables]  ← Custom active

For CUSTOM VARIABLES tab, show a table:
  Columns: Name | Identifier | Type | Source | Fallback | Used in | Actions

  Sample rows:
    - Preferred language | candidate.preferred_language | Text | 
      Candidate field | "English" | 3 templates | ⋯
    - Team lead name | job.team_lead_name | Text | Job field | 
      "your team lead" | 2 templates | ⋯
    - Visa status required | job.visa_required | Yes/No | Job field | 
      "No" | 1 template | ⋯
    - Onboarding buddy | onboarding.buddy_email | Email | Manual entry | 
      "—" | 1 template | ⋯
    - Benefits summary | links.benefits_pdf | Link | Static | 
      "https://connect-ai.com/benefits" | 4 templates | ⋯

For SYSTEM VARIABLES tab, show the same table but read-only with no 
"Actions" column and a note at the top: "System variables are provided 
by Connect AI and cannot be edited."

Clicking "+ New custom variable" opens a side panel (~480px from right) with:
  - Variable name (text)
  - Identifier (auto-generated from name, editable, lowercase with dots/
    underscores, e.g. "candidate.preferred_language")
  - Type (dropdown: Text / Number / Date / Yes-No / Link / Email)
  - Source (dropdown):
      • Candidate field — pick which field
      • Job field — pick which field
      • Manual entry (filled in by recruiter at send time)
      • Static value (fixed for all sends)
  - Fallback value (text)
    Helper: "Used when the data is missing. Always required for safety."
  - "Save variable" + "Cancel" at bottom

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
INTERACTION REQUIREMENTS
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Clicking a template card in View 1 navigates to View 2
- Clicking "Manage variables" navigates to View 3
- Breadcrumb back-links work
- Toolbar buttons in the body editor visually toggle (active/inactive 
  states only — no need for real text formatting)
- Variable picker dropdown opens on "+ Insert variable" click and inserts 
  a variable chip into a sample cursor position
- Sample candidate switcher in preview updates the resolved variable 
  values
- Desktop/Mobile toggle changes preview width
- Tabs switch content
- Auto-save indicator shows "Saving…" briefly when any input changes, 
  then "All changes saved · just now"
- Variable chips in the body should be visually distinct from regular 
  text (purple bg, purple text, small)
- Send test button shows a brief modal: "Send test to: [email input] — 
  Send"

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
NEW VISUAL PATTERNS ALLOWED (consistent with existing style)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Two-column editor + live preview layout
- Variable chips inline in text fields and editor
- Variable picker dropdown panel
- Side panel sliding from right (for creating variables)
- Tab navigation with underline active state
- Border-left accent on template cards in category color
- Soft amber warning state for unresolved variables
- Email-client-style preview mockup

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DO NOT
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT redesign the sidebar, top bar, logo, or color palette
- Do NOT introduce gradients, glassmorphism, or skeuomorphic effects
- Do NOT build a real rich-text editor library — visual toolbar only is fine
- Do NOT add features outside the email scope (no workflow editing, 
  no candidate views, no analytics dashboards)
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults — match the soft-card aesthetic
- Do NOT use emoji as icons except where shown in the email body itself — 
  use lucide-react for all UI icons
- Do NOT add open-rate analytics, A/B testing, or scheduling UI

Match the polish level of the existing Connect AI app. The editor should 
feel as good as Customer.io or Postmark, not Mailchimp's heavy enterprise UI.
</pasted_text>

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (96 lines)">
─────────────────────────────────────────
TEMPLATE CREATION FLOW  (modal)
─────────────────────────────────────────
Triggered by:
  - "+ New template" button in View 1 header
  - "+ Create from scratch" dashed card at the end of "Your templates"
  - "Use as template" / "Duplicate" on any starter or custom card (this 
    skips the modal and goes straight to the editor with content pre-filled)

When triggered, show a centered modal (~560px wide) with backdrop dim:

Modal header:
  Title "Create new email template"
  Subtitle "A few quick details to get you started. You can change 
  everything later."
  Close X in top-right

Modal body, vertical form:

  Field — Template name (required)
    Text input, placeholder "e.g. Final Interview Confirmation"

  Field — Category (required)
    Dropdown with color-coded options matching the library:
    Application / Screening / Interview / Assessment / Rejection / 
    Offer / Onboarding / Internal Communication

  Field — Language (required)
    Segmented control: [English] [العربية]  
    (Default to English. Show small helper: "You can create variants in 
    other languages later from the editor.")

  Field — Start from (required, radio group with cards)
    Three large radio cards in a row:
    
    ○ Blank template
        "Start with empty subject and body. Recommended if you have 
        specific content in mind."
        Document icon
    
    ● Starter template
        "Begin from a Connect AI starter and customize. Recommended 
        for most teams."
        Stack icon
        When selected, reveals a second dropdown below: 
        "Choose a starter…" with filtered list based on category 
        selected above (e.g., if category = Interview, show: 
        Interview Invitation, Interview Reminder, Interview 
        Confirmation, Senior Engineer Technical Brief, etc.)
    
    ○ ✦ Generate with AI
        "Describe what you want to say. AI drafts subject and body 
        with the right variables."
        Sparkle icon (teal accent)
        When selected, reveals a textarea below: 
        "Describe the email in one or two sentences" with placeholder 
        "e.g. Invite the candidate to a 60-minute technical interview 
        with two engineers, mention it's via video call, and include 
        the scheduling link."

  Field — Default recipient (collapsed, "Advanced" expandable section)
    Chip multi-select with defaults based on category:
    - Application/Screening/Interview/Assessment/Offer/Onboarding → 
      [Candidate ✓] by default
    - Internal Communication → [Hiring Manager ✓] by default

Modal footer:
  Right-aligned: "Cancel" ghost button + "Create template" primary 
  purple button

  Validation:
  - "Create template" disabled until name, category, language, and 
    starting choice are all set
  - If "Starter template" selected, the starter dropdown must have a 
    value
  - If "Generate with AI" selected, the description must have at least 
    20 characters

Behavior on submit:
  - Modal closes
  - Navigates to View 2 (template editor) with the new template loaded:
    • Blank → editor opens with default subject "Subject…" and an 
      empty body
    • Starter → editor opens with the starter's subject and body 
      pre-filled (now editable as the org's own copy)
    • AI → editor opens with AI-generated subject and body, plus a 
      small teal banner at the top: "✦ AI-generated draft — review 
      before saving." with a "Regenerate" link
  - The template appears in the library immediately as a draft until 
    first save

When triggered from "Use as template" or "Duplicate" on an existing card:
  - Skip the modal entirely
  - Create a duplicate immediately with name "[Original name] (copy)"
  - Navigate to View 2 with the duplicate loaded
  - Show a small toast: "Template duplicated. Edit and save when ready."
</pasted_text>

_[tool: fork_verifier_agent]_

The **Template Creation Flow** is fully wired. Here's what was added:

**"+ New template" / "Create from scratch"** both open the modal. **"Use as template"** on starter cards and **"Duplicate"** in the kebab skip the modal and go straight to the editor.

**Modal (560px, backdrop dim):**
- **Template name** — required text input
- **Category** — color-coded dropdown that filters the Starter sub-list
- **Language** — segmented EN / AR control with helper note
- **Start from** — three interactive radio cards:
  - **Blank** — opens editor with empty subject + body
  - **Starter** *(default selected)* — reveals a filtered dropdown of matching starters; pre-fills the editor with that starter's content
  - **✦ Generate with AI** — reveals a textarea (20-char minimum); opens editor with AI-authored content
- **Advanced** — collapsible section with default recipient chips
- **Create template** button stays **disabled** until all required fields + the mode-specific sub-requirement (starter chosen / description ≥ 20 chars) are met

**On submit:**
- Modal closes → editor opens with the new template loaded as a **Draft**
- Blank → empty body, placeholder subject
- Starter → pre-filled subject + body (editable copy)
- AI → body seeded from description + a persistent **teal ✦ banner** at the top of the editor: *"AI-generated draft — review before saving"* with a Regenerate link

**Duplicate / Use as template:** creates `[Name] (copy)` immediately and fires the *"Template duplicated. Edit and save when ready."* toast.

LINKED WORKFLOW STAGES  (replaces "Used in workflows" 
bottom strip in View 2)

  - Send mode (pill — "Auto-send" green or "Draft for review" amber)
  - Delay (e.g., "Immediately" / "After 1 hour" / "After 1 business day")
  - Status (pill — "Active" / "Paused")
  - Actions (kebab menu: Edit linkage / Pause / Unlink)

LINK TO STAGE — MODAL FLOW
─────────────────────────────────────────
Triggered by:
  - "+ Link to a stage" button in the Linked workflow stages card
  - "Edit linkage" from the kebab menu (opens with values pre-filled)

Open a centered modal (~640px wide) with backdrop dim:

Modal header:
  Title "Link template to workflow stage"
  Subtitle "This template will send automatically when candidates 
  enter the selected stage(s)."
  Close X in top-right

Modal body, two-column layout:

LEFT COLUMN (50%):
  
  Section "Where should this template fire?"
  
  Step 1 — Pick workflow(s):
    Multi-select with search:
    "Select workflows…" dropdown that opens a checkbox list:
      ☐ Standard Hire (Preset)
      ☑ Engineering — Senior
      ☑ Engineering — Junior  
      ☐ Sales — Account Executive
      ☐ High-Volume / Operational (Preset)
      ☐ Executive Hire (Preset)
      ☐ Internal Transfer (Preset)
      ☐ Internship Program 2026
    
    Selected workflows appear as removable chips above the dropdown:
    [Engineering — Senior ✕] [Engineering — Junior ✕]
    
    Helper text: "You can link this template to multiple workflows 
    at once. We'll show you the stages for each."

  Step 2 — Pick stage(s) within selected workflows:
    Once workflows are picked, show a list of all their stages, 
    grouped by workflow:
    
    Engineering — Senior
      ☐ Applied (Applied)
      ☐ CV Review (Screening)
      ☑ Recruiter Screen (Screening) [already linked — uncheck to remove]
      ☐ Technical Assessment (Assessment) ⊘ Optional
      ☐ Technical Interview (Interview)
      ☐ Final Interview (Interview)
      ☐ Offer (Offer)
      ☐ Hired (Hired, terminal)
      ☐ Rejected (Rejected, terminal)
    
    Engineering — Junior
      ☐ Applied (Applied)
      ☐ CV Review (Screening)
      ☑ Phone Screen (Screening) [already linked]
      ☐ Coding Test (Assessment)
      ☐ Team Interview (Interview)
      ☐ Offer (Offer)
      ☐ Hired (Hired, terminal)
      ☐ Rejected (Rejected, terminal)
    
    Each stage row shows: checkbox, stage name, canonical type chip, 
    optional badge if applicable, and a small note if a different 
    template is already linked to that stage:
    
    ☐ CV Review (Screening) ⚠ "Already linked to 'Application Received'"
    
    Checking such a stage shows an inline confirmation: 
    "Replace 'Application Received' with this template on CV Review?"

  AI suggestion banner (teal accent, at the top of Step 2):
    ✦ "Based on this template's category (Interview), we recommend 
    linking it to stages of type: Screening, Interview"
    [Auto-select recommended stages] link

RIGHT COLUMN (50%):
  
  Section "Linkage settings"
  Helper: "These settings apply to all the stages you select. You can 
  customize per stage after linking."
  
  Recipients (multi-select chips with defaults from template):
    [Candidate ✓] [+ Add recipient]
    Options: Hiring Manager, Recruiter, Assigned Interviewer(s), 
    Custom user
  
  Send mode (radio):
    ● Auto-send immediately
    ○ Create draft for recruiter to review and send
  
  Delay (dropdown):
    "Send immediately" / "After 1 hour" / "After 1 business day" / 
    "Custom…"
  
  Status:
    ● Active   ○ Paused (linkage exists but won't fire)

Modal footer:
  Left side: "Selected: 3 stages across 2 workflows" (live count)
  Right side: "Cancel" ghost + "Link to selected stages" primary purple
  
  Validation:
  - "Link to selected stages" disabled until at least one stage checked
  - If replacing existing linkages, button text changes to:
    "Link to selected stages (replaces 2 existing)"

On submit:
  - Modal closes
  - Bottom strip refreshes with new linkages added
  - Small toast: "Template linked to 3 stages."
  - If replacements occurred, toast adds: "2 previous linkages were 
    replaced."

  - "Change stage" link beside it (opens the picker again)
  - Right column shows only THIS linkage's settings — recipients, 
    send mode, delay, status
  - Footer button changes to "Save changes"

ADD STAGE FLOW  (modal)
─────────────────────────────────────────
Triggered by:
  - "+ Add stage" dashed placeholder card at the end of the pipeline
  - "+" insert affordance between any two adjacent stages on hover
  - "Insert stage" tooltip click

When triggered, show a centered modal (~560px wide) with backdrop dim:

Modal header:
  Title "Add new stage"
  Subtitle "Stages define the steps candidates move through. Pick a 
  template or start blank."
  Close X in top-right

Modal body, vertical form:

  Field — Stage name (required)
    Text input, placeholder "e.g. Technical Interview"
    Helper: "This is what your team sees on the pipeline."

  Field — Stage type (required)
    Dropdown with the canonical types, each with a short description:
      Applied — "Candidates who just applied"
      Screening — "Initial review, recruiter calls, CV screening"
      Interview — "Live interviews with the team"
      Assessment — "Tests, take-homes, technical evaluations"
      Offer — "Offer extended, awaiting response"
      Hired — "Successful hires (terminal)"
      Rejected — "Did not progress (terminal)"
      Other — "Custom stage type"
    
    Helper: "Stage type drives reporting and integrations. The name 
    can be anything you want."

  Field — Insert position (required, radio group)
    ● At the end of the pipeline (before Hired/Rejected)
    ○ After a specific stage…
        When selected, reveals a dropdown listing existing non-terminal 
        stages: "After: [Applied ▾]"

  Field — Required or optional (radio)
    ● Required — "Every candidate must pass through this stage"
    ○ Optional — "Can be skipped per candidate"

  Field — Color accent (5 small color swatches)
    Gray (default), Blue, Purple, Teal, Amber

  Section (collapsed, "Advanced" expandable):
    - "Link an email template now?" toggle
      When ON, opens the template linkage section inline (see 
      TEMPLATE PICKER below) — same UI as Step 2 of the link flow.
    - "Skip this for now" — user can configure email later from the 
      stage side panel.

Modal footer:
  Right-aligned: "Cancel" ghost button + "Add stage" primary purple button
  
  Validation:
  - "Add stage" disabled until name and stage type are set
  - If terminal type (Hired/Rejected) is chosen, helper appears:
    "Terminal stages appear at the end of the pipeline as exit points 
    and cannot be reordered into the middle."

Behavior on submit:
  - Modal closes
  - New stage appears in the canvas with a brief highlight pulse (the 
    new stage glows with a subtle purple ring for 1.5 seconds)
  - Canvas auto-scrolls to bring the new stage into view if it's off-screen
  - Small toast: "Stage added."
  - If email linkage was set in the modal, the stage card immediately 
    shows the mail icon + template name

When triggered from the "+" insert affordance between two stages:
  - "Insert position" field is pre-set to "After [Stage Name]" and 
    is read-only
  - The dropdown can still be changed if user changes their mind

Design a Job Creation flow for "Connect AI", an existing AI-powered HR 
recruitment platform. This is a NEW feature added to a LIVE product — 
match the established visual language exactly. Do not redesign the existing UI.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items have a light lavender background, deep purple 
  text (#6B5BFF), and a thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, dark-mode 
  toggle, notification bell, primary "+ Create" button in solid purple
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF range)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4 range) for AI-related badges
- Typography: clean sans-serif, large bold numbers for metrics
- Soft pastel pill badges with deeper text
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke, minimal (use lucide-react)
- Logo: "Connect AI" + small purple sparkle in dark rounded square
- Sidebar bottom: circular avatar with initial, user name, role title
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English for this design

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WHAT TO BUILD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
A single self-contained React artifact representing a 6-step job creation 
wizard. Use useState to navigate between steps. Use lucide-react for icons.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
GLOBAL WIZARD CHROME (visible on every step except Step 6)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Top header strip:
  Left: Breadcrumb "Jobs › New job"
  Center: Job title preview (e.g., "Senior Frontend Engineer" — appears 
    once entered in Step 1; before that, "Untitled job")
  Right: 
    - "Save and exit" ghost link (saves draft, returns to Jobs list)
    - "Discard" ghost link (red text, confirmation modal)

Horizontal step indicator below the header:
  6 numbered pills, connected by lines. Each pill shows step number, 
  step name, and a state:
    - Completed: filled purple circle with checkmark
    - Active: outlined purple circle with number, deeper text
    - Pending: gray circle with number, lighter text
  
  Completed steps are clickable (returns to that step).
  Pending steps are not clickable.
  
  Step labels:
    1. Basics  →  2. Description  →  3. Evaluation  →  4. Team & Launch  
    →  5. Candidates (optional)  →  6. Review

Below the indicator, a subtle "Auto-saved · just now" or 
"Saving…" indicator on the right.

Main content area: white card, generous padding, max-width ~880px, 
centered.

Footer strip (sticky bottom):
  Left: "← Back" ghost button (disabled on Step 1)
  Right: "Next →" primary purple button (disabled until step is valid)
  On Step 4: "Next →" changes to "Continue to candidates →"
  On Step 5: button reads "Skip — add candidates later" (ghost) 
    + "Continue to review →" (primary)
  On Step 6: "Save as draft" (ghost) + "Publish job" (primary purple)

─────────────────────────────────────────
Page heading: "Let's set up your job"
Subtitle: "Start with the essentials. You can change everything later."

Form, single column with logical grouping:

Group "Role"

    Placeholder: "e.g. Senior Frontend Engineer"

    Options: Engineering, Product, Design, Marketing, Sales, Operations,

  Two columns:
  - Seniority level (dropdown): Intern, Entry, Junior, Mid, Senior,

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
INTERACTION REQUIREMENTS
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Step indicator pills are clickable for completed steps (navigates back)
- "Save and exit" preserves draft state and returns to Jobs list
- AI generate / regenerate buttons show a brief loading state 
  (e.g., "✦ AI is writing…" with a subtle pulse animation)
- Sliders for weights auto-rebalance so total = 100%
- Tier threshold draggable bar updates the numbers below as it moves
- Toggle switches for distribution channels expand to show sub-options 
  when turned on
- "Edit" links on the review step jump back to that step
- File upload zone in Step 5 accepts drag-and-drop (visual only — 
  use a sample file list)
- Auto-save indicator briefly shows "Saving…" then "Auto-saved · just now"
- Footer "Next" buttons enable/disable based on step validation

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DO NOT
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT redesign the sidebar, top bar, logo, or color palette
- Do NOT introduce gradients, glassmorphism, or skeuomorphic effects
- Do NOT block the wizard on async operations (CV parsing happens in 
  the background)
- Do NOT show all six steps' content at once — only the active step 
  is visible
- Do NOT make the user re-enter information across steps
- Do NOT use emoji as icons — use lucide-react throughout
- Do NOT add features outside the job creation scope (no candidate 
  profiles, no scoring UI, no email composer)

Match the polish level of the existing Connect AI app. The wizard 
should feel like a confident, AI-assisted setup experience — not a 
form to fill out.
</pasted_text>

<attached-skill name="Design System (design system)">
[Design System] This project uses the **Design System** design system. This is a binding choice for visual style — every visual must follow it. Don't invent colors, type, spacing, or components not grounded here.

Scope: the design system is a visual style reference only. Its guide may describe example products, brands, or people that are unrelated to the user and unrelated to the subject of this conversation. Never treat anything in the design system as a fact about the user, their work, or the topic they asked about.

    Explore it to find what you need:
    - Always copy out the fonts and colors you need
    - For prototypes and designs, always copy out any relevant components
    - If the design system contains existing mocks of products, and you were asked to design or prototype something similar, copy and fork those mocks to start your design. This helps you make high-quality designs.

    Explore it quickly to find relevant UI kits (e.g. mocks of existing products you can copy and fork)

Full system at `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`. Before producing any visuals, explore it: call `list_files("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/")` to see the structure, then `read_file` the README/base.md or whatever index file it has. Don't guess at the design system's contents.

CSS tokens: the guide may describe tokens in prose, but the exact `--*` names are defined in the design system's stylesheet(s). Before writing any `var(--*)`, look up the real name in the design system's `.css` files (`list_files` + `read_file` under `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`). Never guess a token name — an unresolved `var()` silently falls back to the browser default.

For assets and UI kits beyond the guide: `read_file("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/<path>")` and `copy_files` to bring them into the current project.

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (246 lines)">
Design the candidate profile shell for "Connect AI", an existing 
AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This is a NEW feature added to a 
LIVE product — match the established visual language exactly. Do not 
redesign the existing UI.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, dark-mode 
  toggle, notification bell, primary "+ Create" button in solid purple
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI badges on light teal bg
- Typography: clean sans-serif, large bold numbers for metrics
- Soft pastel pill badges with deeper text
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke (use lucide-react)
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SIDEBAR NAVIGATION (active: Pipeline — unchanged, no new items)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN: Dashboard
HIRING: Jobs (8), Pipeline (64) ← active, Assessments, Video Interviews, 
        Offers (5)
ADMIN: Users (47), Roles, Workflows, Email Templates

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DATA MODEL — IMPORTANT
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The candidate is ONE entity. Ahmed Hassan is one person who may have 
applied to multiple jobs. Each application is a child of the candidate.

The profile shows ONE candidate at a time, with the user choosing which 
APPLICATION'S context to view at any moment. Switching application 
context updates: breadcrumb, mini pipeline, AI score, all tab content, 
and the AI panel's scope. The candidate's CV, contact info, tags, and 
candidate-wide notes are shared across applications.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
PROFILE SHELL (visible on every tab)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

1. BREADCRUMB:
   Reflects the currently selected application context:
   "Pipeline › Senior Frontend Engineer › Ahmed Hassan"

2. TOP HEADER STRIP (white card, sticky, contains 2 sub-rows):
   
   ──── SUB-ROW A — APPLICATION SWITCHER (top of card, low visual weight) ────
   A pill-style strip with light gray background, sitting above the 
   candidate identity row, separated by a thin border-bottom.
   
   Left side:
     - Small gray label "Viewing for:"
     - Dropdown trigger (clickable): 
       "Senior Frontend Engineer · Recruiter Screen ▾"
     - Small purple pill next to trigger: "87 match"
   
   Right side:
     - Small clickable text: "3 applications" (with chevron icon)
   
   Both sides open the same dropdown panel (~360px wide, anchored to 
   the trigger):
   
   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
   │ ACTIVE APPLICATIONS (2)                              │
   │                                                       │
   │ ● Senior Frontend Engineer                            │
   │   Engineering · Recruiter Screen                      │
   │   87 match · Strong   [currently viewing]            │
   │                                                       │
   │ ○ Engineering Manager                                 │
   │   Engineering · Applied                               │
   │   78 match · Good                                     │
   │                                                       │
   │ CLOSED APPLICATIONS (1)                               │
   │                                                       │
   │ ○ Backend Engineer                       [Closed]    │
   │   Engineering · Rejected May 2026                    │
   │   52 match · Weak                                     │
   │                                                       │
   │ ─────────────────────────────────────────────         │
   │ ↗ View candidate-wide summary                         │
   │ + Add Ahmed to a new job                              │
   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
   
   - Active applications listed first, closed below with reduced opacity
   - Currently-viewed application has filled radio dot and pill label
   - Clicking any other entry switches application context
   - Bottom footer items navigate to other surfaces
   - If candidate has only one application, the application switcher 
     simplifies to: "Viewing for: Senior Frontend Engineer · 1 application"
     (no dropdown, just a label)
   
   ──── SUB-ROW B — CANDIDATE IDENTITY (the main header content) ────
   Left:
     - 48px avatar circle (initials "AH" on light purple bg, #EEEDFE)
     - Below avatar OR to the right: 
       - Name "Ahmed Hassan" (16px, weight 500)
       - "Strong match" pill (purple bg #EEEDFE, purple text #3C3489)
       - Sub-line (12px gray): "Applied: Senior Frontend Engineer · 
         4 days ago · Riyadh, KSA"
   
   Right:
     - Lens toggle (small segmented control): [Full] [Interview] [Manager]
       - "Full" is selected by default
     - Primary purple button: "Move to Technical Interview" with 
       dropdown chevron (application-scoped action)
     - Ghost icon button: three-dot kebab for more actions

3. MINI PIPELINE STRIP (white card, full width, sticky below header):
   Application-scoped — reflects the workflow of the currently viewed 
   application.
   
   Horizontal stage flow with chevron separators:
   Applied › CV Review › [Recruiter Screen] (purple highlighted pill) › 
   Technical Interview › Final Interview › Offer › Hired
   Right side: "⏱ 3 days in stage" small gray text

4. THREE-COLUMN LAYOUT (below shell):
   - LEFT RAIL (280px sticky): see section 6 below
   - MAIN CONTENT (flex, varies by tab — tab-specific design)
   - RIGHT RAIL (340px sticky): Ask AI panel + Similar candidates + 
     Quick actions (always visible across all tabs; details in 
     separate prompt for Ask AI)

5. TAB BAR (above main content, below shell):
   Horizontal tabs with underline-active state:
   [Overview] CV & Parsing | Assessment | Video Interview | 
   Evaluations (0/3) | Emails (5) | Notes (2) | Activity
   
   Each tab's counts and content are application-scoped — switching 
   application context updates tab counts.

6. LEFT RAIL — three stacked cards (always visible):

   ──── CARD A: COMPOSITE AI MATCH (application-scoped) ────
   White card at top of left rail.
   "✦ AI MATCH" small caps label
   Large purple number: 87/100
   Tier badge: "Strong match"
   "High confidence" small gray text
   
   Below the score, a small list "Signals contributing:":
     ● CV match           9.0
     ● Pre-screen         8.5
     ● Assessment         8.7
     ○ Video interview    —
     ○ Human evaluation   —
   (filled dot = signal received, hollow dot = pending)
   
   Small "How is this calculated?" link at the bottom (teal).
   
   ──── CARD B: CANDIDATE INFO (candidate-wide, shared across applications) ────
   White card.
   Sub-label: "Candidate" (small caps, gray)
   Rows with icons:
     📍 Riyadh, KSA
     💼 6 years experience
     🗣 English only
     🔗 LinkedIn profile
   
   ──── CARD C: STRENGTHS (application-scoped) ────
   White card.
   Header: "Strengths" with small up-arrow icon
   Three bullets:
     • Deep React expertise (6 yrs)
     • Led team of 4 engineers
     • Fintech background
   
   ──── CARD D: CONCERNS (application-scoped) ────
   White card.
   Header: "Concerns" with small alert icon (amber)
   Two bullets:
     • No Arabic communication
     • Limited backend exposure
   
   ──── CARD E: TAGS (candidate-wide, shared) ────
   White card.
   Header: "Tags"
   Tag chips:
     [Bilingual] [Fintech] [Remote-OK]
   
   ──── CARD F: OTHER APPLICATIONS (NEW — only shown if candidate has 
        more than 1 application) ────
   White card.
   Header: "Other applications" + count badge "2"
   
   List of other applications (excluding currently viewed):
   
     Engineering Manager
     Applied · 78 · Good
     
     Backend Engineer                              [Closed]
     Rejected · 52 · Weak
   
   Active apps: full opacity. Closed apps: 70% opacity + "Closed" pill.
   Each row clickable — switches application context.
   
   Footer: "View all 3 →" link (teal)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SWITCHING APPLICATION CONTEXT — BEHAVIOR
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
When user switches application context (via switcher dropdown OR via 
"Other applications" card OR via any "switch context" link):

1. Breadcrumb updates to the new job title
2. Mini pipeline strip updates to the new application's workflow and 
   current stage
3. Left rail AI Match score updates (signals + total + tier)
4. Left rail Strengths and Concerns cards update (application-scoped)
5. Left rail "Other applications" card updates to exclude the new 
   active application and include the previously active one
6. All tab content updates to reflect the new application's data
7. Tab counts update (Emails count, Evaluations count, Notes count, etc.)
8. Right rail Ask AI panel scope changes (AI now has context of new app)
9. URL updates in the background (e.g., /jobs/eng-manager/candidates/
   ahmed-hassan), but visually feels like staying on the same profile
10. A small toast appears at the bottom: 
    "Switched to Engineering Manager application"

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
PERMISSIONS BEHAVIOR
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
If the recruiter has access to some of Ahmed's applications but not 
others, the application switcher dropdown still shows all applications 
by title and stage, but inaccessible ones are visually muted, marked 
"Restricted access," and unclickable. This keeps the candidate-centric 
model honest while respecting permission boundaries.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DO NOT
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT redesign the sidebar, top bar, logo, or color palette
- Do NOT add new sidebar items
- Do NOT introduce gradients, glassmorphism, or skeuomorphic effects
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults
- Do NOT use emoji as icons — use lucide-react
- Do NOT add a footer
- Do NOT split the candidate into multiple records — one candidate, 
  one profile, multiple applications viewable in context
</pasted_text>

<attached-skill name="Design System (design system)">
[Design System] This project uses the **Design System** design system. This is a binding choice for visual style — every visual must follow it. Don't invent colors, type, spacing, or components not grounded here.

Scope: the design system is a visual style reference only. Its guide may describe example products, brands, or people that are unrelated to the user and unrelated to the subject of this conversation. Never treat anything in the design system as a fact about the user, their work, or the topic they asked about.

    Explore it to find what you need:
    - Always copy out the fonts and colors you need
    - For prototypes and designs, always copy out any relevant components
    - If the design system contains existing mocks of products, and you were asked to design or prototype something similar, copy and fork those mocks to start your design. This helps you make high-quality designs.

    Explore it quickly to find relevant UI kits (e.g. mocks of existing products you can copy and fork)

Full system at `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`. Before producing any visuals, explore it: call `list_files("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/")` to see the structure, then `read_file` the README/base.md or whatever index file it has. Don't guess at the design system's contents.

CSS tokens: the guide may describe tokens in prose, but the exact `--*` names are defined in the design system's stylesheet(s). Before writing any `var(--*)`, look up the real name in the design system's `.css` files (`list_files` + `read_file` under `/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/`). Never guess a token name — an unresolved `var()` silently falls back to the browser default.

For assets and UI kits beyond the guide: `read_file("/projects/e5b2401a-4d06-40b2-b53b-78bca8727081/<path>")` and `copy_files` to bring them into the current project.
</attached-skill>

- Just **3 stages**: Applied → then the two terminal end-caps (✓ Hired / ✗ Rejected)
- **0 candidates**, no email links, no prefilled content

From there you can use **+ Add stage** cards and the **+** insert affordances between stages to build the workflow from scratch. Each stage opens the config panel when clicked.

12.1 — Assessment Library Management
US-12.1.1 — As an HR Admin, I want a centralized assessment library, so that recruiters can browse and assign pre-built assessments without building from scratch.

AC: Library is organized by type (Technical / Functional / Psychometric) and by domain (e.g. Programming, Finance, Personality)
AC: Each assessment shows: title, type, domain, estimated duration, difficulty level, number of questions, last updated date
AC: HR Admin can filter by type, domain, difficulty, and duration
AC: Library is scoped to the organization — assessments are not shared across tenants
AC: System ships with a default question bank per domain (minimum 50 questions per domain at launch)

US-12.1.2 — As an HR Admin, I want to create a custom assessment from scratch, so that I can test skills specific to our organization.

AC: Form accepts: title, type, domain, instructions, time limit (optional), pass mark (optional)
AC: Questions can be added manually or pulled from the library question bank
AC: Supported question types: multiple choice, multi-select, true/false, short answer, long answer, code challenge (technical only), file upload (functional only), Likert scale (psychometric only)
AC: Preview mode shows the assessment exactly as the candidate will see it
AC: Assessment is saved as draft until explicitly published

US-12.1.3 — As an HR Admin, I want to use AI to generate an assessment from a job description, so that the questions are role-relevant without manual effort.

AC: Input: paste JD or select an existing job from the platform
AC: AI generates a recommended assessment with: suggested type mix, question count, time limit, and sample questions
AC: HR Admin can accept, edit, or regenerate any section before saving
AC: Generation completes in ≤15 seconds for 95% of requests
AC: Generated assessment is saved as draft for review before publishing

US-12.1.4 — As an HR Admin, I want to version assessments, so that changes don't affect candidates already in progress.

AC: Editing a published assessment creates a new version (v1, v2, etc.)
AC: In-progress candidate sessions always use the version they were sent
AC: HR Admin can view all versions and their usage stats
AC: Deprecated versions cannot be assigned to new candidates but remain accessible for historical results


12.2 — Assessment Assignment &amp; Distribution
US-12.2.1 — As a Recruiter, I want to assign an assessment to a candidate from their profile, so that I can evaluate skills at the right pipeline stage.

AC: "Send Assessment" action available on every candidate profile and from the pipeline board
AC: Recruiter selects from the published assessment library (filterable by type and domain)
AC: Recruiter sets: deadline (default 5 days), reminder schedule (default: 24h before deadline), optional personal message
AC: Candidate receives an email with a unique, single-use assessment link
AC: Assessment status appears on the candidate profile: Not Sent / Invited / In Progress / Submitted / Expired / Scored

US-12.2.2 — As a Recruiter, I want to assign assessments automatically when a candidate reaches a pipeline stage, so that I don't have to trigger it manually.

AC: Stage transition automation (from Epic 8) supports "send assessment" as a trigger action
AC: Recruiter selects which assessment to send in the workflow configuration
AC: Auto-assignment respects the same deadline and reminder defaults as manual assignment
AC: If a candidate already has a submitted result for the same assessment, auto-assignment is skipped and existing result is flagged

US-12.2.3 — As a Recruiter, I want to send the same assessment to multiple candidates at once, so that I can screen a large applicant pool efficiently.

AC: Bulk select candidates from the pipeline board (up to 50 at a time)
AC: Single assessment selection applied to all selected candidates
AC: Individual deadlines can be overridden per candidate before sending
AC: Bulk send confirmation shows a summary before dispatching
AC: Failed sends (invalid email, expired candidate) listed in a send report

US-12.2.4 — As a Recruiter, I want to track assessment completion status across all candidates for a job, so that I know who has responded.

AC: Assessment status column available on the pipeline board
AC: Filter pipeline by assessment status (e.g. show all "Invited" or "Expired")
AC: Overdue candidates (past deadline, not submitted) highlighted in amber
AC: One-click reminder send for overdue candidates
</pasted_text>

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (60 lines)">
Add the following new epic and user stories to the assessment backlog.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EPIC 12.3 — Candidate Experience
Goal: Deliver a clean, fair, accessible test-taking experience for 
candidates regardless of whether they have a Connect AI account.
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

US-12.3.1 — As a Candidate, I want to receive a clear assessment invitation by email, so that I understand what's expected before I start.

AC: Email contains: company name, role applied for, assessment name, type, estimated duration, deadline, and a unique single-use link
AC: Email respects the candidate's preferred language (English or Arabic) if known; otherwise uses the assessment's primary language
AC: Email is sent from a verified company sender address (per Connect AI's email infrastructure)
AC: Email link remains valid until the assessment deadline; expired links route to a "This assessment has expired" page with recruiter contact info
AC: Reminder emails are sent per schedule configured by the recruiter

US-12.3.2 — As a Candidate, I want to access the assessment without creating a Connect AI account, so that I can focus on the test, not paperwork.

AC: The unique link authenticates the candidate; no signup, login, or password required
AC: Link is single-use; if a candidate attempts to share the link, the system flags the second access and notifies the recruiter
AC: Link works on Chrome, Safari, Firefox (latest two versions of each), on desktop and mobile
AC: If the candidate accesses the link from a device with no microphone/camera/JavaScript support, they see a clear message about minimum requirements

US-12.3.3 — As a Candidate, I want to see clear pre-test instructions and honor code, so that I know exactly what to expect.

AC: Landing page shows: assessment name, duration, number of questions, sections (if applicable), attempt limit, language options (if multi-variant)
AC: Page lists what is and isn't allowed (external resources, AI tools, etc.) as a numbered "Before you start" list
AC: Page displays an honor code that the candidate must explicitly accept (checkbox) before the "Start" button is enabled
AC: Honor code acceptance is timestamped and stored as part of the submission record
AC: Candidate can choose language (English / Arabic / other configured variants) before starting; selection persists for the duration of the test

US-12.3.4 — As a Candidate, I want to take the test with confidence in the technology, so that I focus on the questions and not the tooling.

AC: Timer is visible at all times when a time limit is set; visual treatment intensifies as time runs low (e.g. amber under 5 minutes)
AC: Every answer is auto-saved within 5 seconds of the last interaction; an indicator confirms save status
AC: Connection loss is detected; the candidate sees a banner and the test pauses; on reconnection, they resume from the last saved state
AC: Navigation depends on test settings: per-question forward-only, OR free navigation between questions within a section, OR free navigation throughout
AC: Section progress and overall progress are visible
AC: Candidate can flag a question for review (if back-navigation is allowed) and see flagged questions in a summary at the end

US-12.3.5 — As a Candidate, I want a clear submission confirmation, so that I know my work is complete.

AC: On submit, a confirmation page shows: assessment name, submission timestamp, time taken, questions answered, and a confirmation ID
AC: Confirmation email is sent to the candidate's address with the same details
AC: Page describes what happens next ("the team will review within X business days")
AC: Candidate cannot re-access the assessment link after submission

US-12.3.6 — As a Candidate, I want to resume a paused or interrupted assessment from the same email link, so that I don't lose progress.

AC: Returning to the link after a pause shows a "Resume" screen with progress summary
AC: Resume preserves: current question, all saved answers, remaining time (if hard timer), and section state
AC: Hard-timer assessments do NOT pause the timer on disconnect; soft-timer assessments DO pause
AC: Resume is allowed up until the deadline; after deadline, the link expires regardless of resume state

US-12.3.7 — As a Candidate, I want the test to work in Arabic with proper right-to-left layout, so that I'm not disadvantaged by language.

AC: All UI elements (timer, buttons, navigation, progress, error messages) render correctly in Arabic
AC: Question content, options, and code snippets respect the question author's language variant
AC: Mixed-language content (e.g. English code in an Arabic question) renders directionally correct
AC: Submission and confirmation flows work identically in both languages
</pasted_text>

Built **Epic 12.3 — Candidate Experience** as a full-screen, account-free, bilingual test-taking flow. Launch it from any assessment's detail page via the **"Candidate view"** button. It covers all seven stories:

**12.3.1 — Invitation email** — Rendered email preview from a verified sender with company, role, assessment name, type, duration, deadline, and a single-use link note. Demo buttons jump to the expired-link page (with recruiter contact) and the resume screen.

**12.3.3 — Pre-test landing + honor code** — Shows duration, question count, attempts, language; a numbered "Before you start" allowed/not-allowed list; a language picker (English / العربية) that persists; and an honor-code checkbox that gates the Start button (acceptance is timestamped into the submission record).

**12.3.4 — Taking the test** — Always-visible timer that turns amber under 5 minutes; autosave indicator (Saving… → Saved); a "Simulate offline" control that shows the connection-lost banner and pauses a soft timer (hard timers keep running); progress bar; flag-for-review (when back-nav is allowed); and all question types render as candidate inputs (MCQ, multi, true/false, short/long, code, file upload max 25MB, Likert).

**12.3.5 — Submission confirmation** — Confirmation page with assessment name, submit timestamp, time taken, questions answered, and a unique Confirmation ID; "what happens next" note; and a statement that the link can no longer be used.

**12.3.6 — Resume** — "Welcome back" screen with a progress summary and the timer-pause rules (hard timers don't pause on disconnect; soft timers do).

**12.3.7 — Arabic RTL** — The demo toolbar toggles language live; the entire candidate UI (timer, nav, progress, banners, honor code, confirmation) flips to RTL with IBM Plex Sans Arabic, while code blocks stay LTR.

A small demo toolbar (top corner) lets you toggle language and close — handy for walking stakeholders through both languages without leaving the screen.
