<pasted_text name="Pasted text (65 lines)">
Add the following new epic and user stories to the assessment backlog.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EPIC 12.4 — Grading and Results
Goal: Turn candidate submissions into trustworthy, explainable scores 
that surface in the right places and feed downstream evaluation.
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

US-12.4.1 — As a System, I want to auto-grade objective question types on submission, so that recruiters see scores immediately.

AC: Auto-graded question types: multiple choice, multi-select, true/false, Likert scale
AC: Each question's correct answer(s) are defined at authoring time
AC: Multi-select questions support partial credit per recruiter configuration (off by default)
AC: Score per section is calculated as sum of points; overall score is the sum across sections
AC: Score appears on the candidate profile within 30 seconds of submission
AC: Score is presented as raw points, percentage, and tier (Strong / Good / Possible / Weak based on configurable thresholds)

US-12.4.2 — As a Recruiter, I want AI to grade subjective submissions against a rubric, so that I get a defensible first-pass evaluation without doing every review from scratch.

AC: AI grades: short answer, long answer, file uploads (text, PDF, DOCX content)
AC: Grading uses the rubric defined at assessment authoring time (per-criterion weight + description)
AC: AI output per criterion: score (0-10), evidence citation (specific text in the submission), confidence indicator
AC: AI generates an overall summary explaining strengths, weaknesses, and a recommendation tier
AC: AI grading is clearly marked as a DRAFT until the recruiter confirms; never auto-finalized
AC: AI grading completes in ≤30 seconds for typical text submissions; longer for file content (with progress indicator)
AC: If AI confidence is low for any criterion, the rubric row is flagged for mandatory human review

US-12.4.3 — As a Recruiter, I want to review and override AI grading, so that I have final authority on the score.

AC: Results page shows AI draft score alongside an empty "Recruiter score" override input
AC: Recruiter can adjust individual criterion scores; the overall score recomputes automatically
AC: Recruiter can add a justification note (required if override differs from AI by more than 2 points on any criterion)
AC: Recruiter actions: "Confirm AI score", "Save override", "Reject submission with feedback", "Request team discussion"
AC: Confirming or overriding a score moves the assessment status from "Submitted" to "Scored"
AC: The final score (AI-confirmed or recruiter-overridden) is the one that feeds downstream

US-12.4.4 — As a Recruiter, I want assessment results visible on the candidate profile, so that I see all evaluation signals in one place.

AC: The candidate profile's "Assessment" tab shows every assessment sent and its current status
AC: Completed assessments display: overall score, tier, time taken, per-section breakdown, AI summary, and recruiter notes
AC: Clicking a completed assessment opens the full Results Review screen
AC: Pending and expired assessments are listed with appropriate status pills and quick actions (send reminder, extend deadline, cancel)
AC: Results contribute to the candidate's composite AI Match score (see US-12.4.5)

US-12.4.5 — As a System, I want assessment scores to feed into the candidate's composite AI Match, so that hiring decisions are based on all signals.

AC: When a new assessment score is finalized (confirmed or overridden), the candidate's composite AI Match recalculates
AC: The Signal Timeline on the candidate profile shows the assessment as a contributing signal with its score
AC: If a rubric or weighting is changed after an assessment is scored, the score is NOT retroactively changed; only future submissions use the new logic
AC: Composite calculation logic is documented and accessible via "How is this calculated?" link

US-12.4.6 — As a Recruiter, I want to compare a candidate's assessment results to other candidates for the same job, so that I can calibrate decisions.

AC: Results page shows the candidate's score vs the distribution of all candidates who took the same assessment for the same job (n ≥ 3)
AC: Percentile and rank shown (e.g. "Top 20% · 3 of 14")
AC: Strongest and weakest sections relative to the cohort highlighted
AC: For confidentiality, no other candidate names or scores are shown — only distribution

US-12.4.7 — As a Recruiter, I want to drill into individual question responses, so that I can verify AI grading and spot patterns.

AC: Results page has a "Question-level review" view showing every question and the candidate's answer
AC: For MCQ-type questions: correct answer highlighted, candidate's answer marked correct/incorrect, time spent shown
AC: For subjective questions: candidate's full response shown alongside the AI's per-criterion scoring and evidence citations
AC: Recruiter can leave a comment on any individual question (visible to hiring team)
AC: Question-level data is exportable as PDF for hiring panel discussion
</pasted_text>

Built **Epic 12.4 — Grading and Results** as a full **Results Review** screen. Open it from a published assessment's **Results tab → "Open results review"**, or from a candidate profile's Assessment tab → "Results review". Four tabs cover all seven stories:

**Overview (12.4.1)** — Auto-graded objective score as a ring (raw points / percentage / tier / time taken), section breakdown bars, and the AI evaluation summary (marked **Draft** until scored). A right-hand scoring panel shows **AI draft vs Recruiter** weighted scores side by side, plus the **Composite AI Match** feed (84 → 87 on finalize) with a "How is this calculated?" modal (12.4.5).

**AI rubric grading (12.4.2)** — Per-criterion cards (weight, AI score 0–10, **evidence citation** quoting the submission, **confidence chip**). The low-confidence "Edge-case handling" row is red-flagged for mandatory human review, and the tab shows a warning dot.

**Override (12.4.3)** — Each criterion has a slider + numeric stepper for the recruiter score; the overall recomputes live. Moving more than 2 points from the AI triggers a **required justification** field, and "Save override" stays disabled until it's filled. Action set: Confirm AI score / Save override / Reject with feedback (modal) / Discuss — any of which flips status **Submitted → Scored**.

**Cohort comparison (12.4.6)** — Distribution bar chart with the candidate's band highlighted, **Top 20% · 3 of 14** percentile/rank, and strongest/weakest sections vs the cohort — no other candidate names or scores shown.

**Question-level review (12.4.7)** — Every question with the candidate's answer: MCQ shows correct answer highlighted + correct/incorrect + time spent; subjective shows the full response (code stays LTR) alongside AI per-criterion scores; a per-question comment field for the hiring team; and an Export PDF action.

**Profile integration (12.4.4)** — The candidate Assessment tab now has a "Results review" button on completed assessments that deep-links into this screen.

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (88 lines)">
Add the following two new epics and their user stories to the 
assessment backlog.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EPIC 12.5 — Third-Party Assessment Integrations
Goal: Support specialized assessment types (coding, psychometric) via 
integrated providers while keeping all results, scoring, and decisions 
inside Connect AI.
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

US-12.5.1 — As an HR Admin, I want to connect a third-party assessment provider, so that we can offer specialized assessments without building them in-house.

AC: Integrations page lists available providers: HackerRank, CodeSignal, Codility, Pymetrics, SHL, Hogan, Coderbyte, TestGorilla (initial set)
AC: Connecting a provider requires: API key (or OAuth), confirmation of which tests to expose in the library, default settings (sync mode, score mapping)
AC: Connection status visible: Connected (green) / Error (red, with reason) / Syncing (amber)
AC: At least one integration shipped at launch (recommended: HackerRank for coding)

US-12.5.2 — As a Recruiter, I want external assessments to appear in the library labeled with their provider, so that I know how they'll behave.

AC: External assessments show a "Powered by [Provider]" label in the library
AC: External assessments have a small plug icon next to their type pill
AC: Filtering by type includes external assessments under "Coding" or "Psychometric" buckets

US-12.5.3 — As a Recruiter, I want sending an external assessment to feel identical to sending an in-house one, so that I don't have to learn separate flows.

AC: "Send assessment" flow works the same for external assessments — same picker, same deadline, same email
AC: Candidate receives a Connect AI-branded email; the assessment link routes to the provider's platform
AC: Co-branded experience where the provider supports it (Connect AI logo + provider's test UI)
AC: If the provider doesn't support co-branding, the candidate is informed they're being routed externally

US-12.5.4 — As a System, I want external results to sync back into Connect AI, so that recruiters see them in the candidate profile alongside in-house results.

AC: When the candidate completes an external assessment, results sync to Connect AI within 5 minutes
AC: Synced results contain: overall score, per-section breakdown (where provided), submission timestamp, candidate confirmation
AC: For coding assessments, code submissions are linked back (read-only) with a "View on [Provider]" link
AC: Results appear in the candidate profile's Assessment tab identically to in-house results — same UI, same scoring tier
AC: Sync failures are logged and visible in the integrations admin panel; recruiter receives a notification if a sync fails for more than 24 hours

US-12.5.5 — As an HR Admin, I want to disconnect a provider safely, so that historical data is preserved.

AC: Disconnect action requires explicit confirmation with a summary of impact: which tests will be removed from library, how many in-progress assessments are affected, how many historical results will be preserved
AC: Disconnecting stops new sync but preserves all historical synced data
AC: In-progress assessments at time of disconnect: the candidate can still complete on the provider's platform, but results will NOT sync back; recruiter is warned
AC: Reconnecting a previously connected provider restores library entries automatically

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EPIC 12.6 — Trust Signals and Anti-Cheating
Goal: Provide enough signal that recruiters trust assessment results, 
without building heavy proctoring (which is out of scope for V1).
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

US-12.6.1 — As a Candidate, I want to explicitly accept an honor code before starting, so that the company knows I'm taking the test in good faith.

AC: Honor code is displayed on the pre-test landing page (per US-12.3.3)
AC: Candidate must check a "I agree" box; the Start button is disabled until checked
AC: Honor code content is customizable per organization (admin setting); ships with a default
AC: Acceptance is timestamped and stored as part of the submission record
AC: Honor code text is visible to the recruiter on the results page

US-12.6.2 — As a System, I want to log basic tab-focus events during an active assessment, so that recruiters have signal on possible distraction or cheating.

AC: Tab-switch events are logged: timestamp, duration of switch, whether it was the candidate's tab going inactive or another tab gaining focus
AC: No more than 1 event per second is recorded (debounced)
AC: Events are visible on the results page in an "Activity during the test" section
AC: System does NOT block the candidate from switching tabs — this is signal, not enforcement
AC: Candidate is informed at the start that tab-switch events are logged (per honor code transparency)

US-12.6.3 — As a System, I want to log copy-paste events during an active assessment, so that recruiters can detect external resource use.

AC: Copy events from the assessment page are logged (timestamp, length of copied text)
AC: Paste events into answer fields are logged (timestamp, length of pasted text, whether it matches recent copy)
AC: Events are visible on the results page in the "Activity during the test" section
AC: For code-related questions, copy-paste from documentation sites is expected; the system flags excessive pasting (&gt;500 chars at once) but does not block
AC: Candidate is informed of copy-paste logging via the honor code

US-12.6.4 — As a System, I want to flag submissions with unusual patterns, so that recruiters can verify suspicious results.

AC: Pattern flags include: completion time more than 50% faster than median for the assessment, large pasted blocks not present in the source materials, multiple devices used (different IPs/user agents)
AC: Flags are advisory only — the system does NOT auto-reject flagged submissions
AC: Flagged submissions show an amber indicator on the results page with a "Why was this flagged?" explanation
AC: Recruiter can dismiss flags after review

US-12.6.5 — As a Recruiter, I want all trust signals visible on the results page in one section, so that I can quickly assess submission integrity.

AC: Results page has a dedicated "Trust signals" or "Submission integrity" section
AC: Section shows: honor code accepted (Yes/No, timestamp), tab switches (count), copy-paste events (count, with details on click), total time vs median, device consistency, any flagged patterns
AC: Each signal has a small explanation icon clarifying what it means
AC: Section uses neutral language — these are signals, not accusations
</pasted_text>

**Epic 12.5 — Third-Party Integrations**
- **Integrations admin view** (Assessment Library header → "Integrations"): provider cards for HackerRank, CodeSignal, Codility, Coderbyte, TestGorilla, SHL, Pymetrics, Hogan — each with kind (Coding/Psychometric/Mixed), co-branding flag, and live status pills (Connected / Syncing / Error-with-reason / Not connected). **Epic 12.6 — Trust Signals & Anti-Cheating**

Each card has an info affordance opening a detail modal; flagged patterns show a "Why?" explanation and a Dismiss action. An advisory amber flag pill also appears in the results header and jumps to this tab.

All advisory only — nothing blocks the candidate or auto-rejects.

existing AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This is a NEW feature 
added to a LIVE product — match the established visual language exactly.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell, primary "+ Create" button
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI-related badges
- Typography: clean sans-serif, large bold numbers for metrics
- Soft pastel pill badges with deeper text
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke (use lucide-react)
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English

      EU AI Act and other regulations restrict behavioral inference.")
    ○ Content + voice analysis (disabled)

  "Apply stricter rules for candidates in:"

  Sub-text: "Required for compliance. Cannot be disabled."

White card — "Right to challenge":
  Toggle: "Allow candidates to challenge AI evaluation" [ON]
  Sub-text: "Adds a link in the candidate's confirmation email to 
  request human review."

    1. Want to finish later? Your call link is still valid for the 
       next 48 hours.
       [Resume call →] (primary)
    2. Want to schedule a call with a human instead? 
       [Request human screening →]
    3. Want to withdraw your application? 
       [Withdraw application] (small, gray)

- All other links are visual only (career page, blog, contact)
- Confirmation ID is selectable for copying

- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults

rights. No surprises later.

how can I create a new screening call and link it to a particular opening position

## Assistant

Honestly — that explicit flow isn't built yet. Right now the screening agent is **scoped to a job** (the config screen reads "Screening Agent for Senior Frontend Engineer"), but there's no UI to *create* a new one and pick which opening it belongs to. The Live Monitoring and config screens assume the link already exists.

The natural way to add it, matching patterns already in the app:

1. **From the Screening Calls screen** — a "+ New screening agent" button opening a modal: pick a **Job** (dropdown of open positions), name it, choose a starting point (blank / clone an existing agent / AI-generate goals from that job's JD), then land in the config screen scoped to that job.
2. **Auto-trigger via Workflow** — same pattern as the assessment auto-assign I built into the workflow stage panel: a "Start AI screening call" action on a stage, so candidates reaching e.g. "Recruiter Screen" get the call automatically. This is what actually links calls to a position's pipeline.
3. **From a Job page** — a "Screening" setting on the job itself that enables/links the agent.

Want me to build it? I'd suggest the **"+ New screening agent" modal** (job picker + blank/clone/AI-generate) on the Screening Calls screen as the primary create-and-link flow, plus optionally the workflow "Start screening call" trigger for auto-assignment. Tell me which and I'll wire it.

  Small light-gray strip with:

        we'll add them as knockout questions automatically."

      Sub-header: "Add facts specific to this job that the AI can 
      answer when candidates ask."

        • Salary range: "SAR 22,000 – 28,000 / month" 
          (From job's rubric)
          [Edit] [Remove]
        • Day-to-day: "You'll work on the customer-facing dashboard..."
          [Edit] [Remove]
        + Add knowledge base entry
      
      Below: 
        Toggle: "Pull from job's JD automatically" [ON]
    
    ▾ Custom screening goals (collapsed):
      Sub-header: "Add screening goals specific to this job's rubric."
      
      List of overrides:
        + Pull from job's rubric automatically (toggle)
        + Custom goals (manual)
    
    ▾ Agent style overrides (collapsed):
      Tone, length, language preference — override the template's 
      defaults if needed for this job.

  Header: "Linkage summary"
  Body:
    "✦ This agent will run for candidates who reach the Screening 
    Call stage of Senior Frontend Engineer. It uses the base 
    template 'Connect AI Senior FE Screen' with 2 job-specific

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
INTERACTION
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Toggle buttons at top of artifact switch between Views A, B, C
- In any view, clicking the relevant button opens the LINKAGE MODAL
- The modal's content adapts based on entry context (description 
  changes; some fields hidden if already known)
- "+ Add knockout question" / "+ Add knowledge base entry" opens 
  inline editors
- Toggles "Pull from job automatically" auto-populate the list
- "Preview the call" opens a sample call simulation
- "Unlink" requires confirmation
- "Replace agent" opens a picker similar to the wizard's step 2

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DATA MODEL CLARIFICATION (visible to designers, not users)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
When a job is linked to an agent:
  - The agent template is SNAPSHOT-LINKED to the job, not REFERENCED
  - Job-specific overrides are stored separately as a customization layer
  - At runtime, the active configuration is the template + the 
    customization layer
  - If the template is updated later, the job gets a "Template 
    updated — review changes?" notification (not auto-applied)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DO NOT
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT auto-apply template updates to linked jobs
- Do NOT lose track of which job-specific customizations exist when 
  switching templates
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults
- Do NOT use emoji as icons — use lucide-react

The linkage modal is the most-used administrative flow for screening 
agents. Make it feel like a clean handshake between two existing 
objects — not a setup wizard.
</pasted_text>

The "Link screening agent to job" flow is built with all three entry points converging on a shared linkage modal:

- **View A — Job creation wizard (Step 3):** an "AI Screening Call" card (off by default) that expands to three radio cards (Generate / Pick from library / Start from starter), a "Customize for this job" toggle, and "Set job-specific overrides" → opens the linkage modal in `wizard` mode.
- **View B — Workflow stage panel:** a new "Screening Agent" tab on screening/assessment stages showing the current linked agent (or empty state), job-specific overrides, and template-sync status; Link/Edit/Replace open the modal in `workflow` mode.
- **View C — Linked jobs management** (`screening-linked` route, reached from the library's "Linked to X jobs" link): a table of linked jobs with status, stage, linked-since, override counts, and Edit/Unlink (with confirmation); "+ Link to another job" opens the modal in `agent` mode.

The **shared modal** adapts its title and CTA per entry, shows job context (read-only) or a job picker, three expandable override sections (knockout questions, knowledge base, goals, style) with "pull from job automatically" toggles, and a Template → Job layer → Active summary strip — reinforcing the snapshot-plus-customization-layer model (template updates never auto-apply).

## User

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (516 lines)">
Design the PIPELINE screen for "Connect AI", an existing AI-powered HR 
recruitment platform. The pipeline is where recruiters manage candidates 
across stages — their daily workspace. The product has an existing 
pipeline implementation; this design refines and extends it without 
redesigning the visual language.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI-related badges
- Pastel chip pills with colored text: purple, teal, amber, gray
- Typography: clean sans-serif
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke (use lucide-react)
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SIDEBAR NAVIGATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN: Dashboard
HIRING: Jobs (8), Pipeline (64) ← ACTIVE, Assessments, 
        Video Interviews, Screening Calls, Offers (5)
ADMIN: Users (47), Roles, Workflows, Email Templates

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
PAGE HEADER (sticky at top)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Title row:
  Left:
    Title "Pipeline" (28px, weight 600)
    Sub-line (12px, gray): "Drag candidates between stages · AI-ranked"
  
  Right side (cluster of controls):
    - Search input: "Search candidates..." (with search icon)
      Width: ~280px, sticky in the header
    - Job picker dropdown (matches existing pattern):
      "All jobs ▾" (current default)
      Opens a dropdown showing:
        ✓ All jobs (selected)
        ───────────────────
        Senior Product Manager
        Senior Frontend Engineer
        Data Scientist
        Financial Analyst
        Growth Marketing Lead
        + 3 more
      Dropdown width: ~280px
    - View toggle (segmented control): [Kanban ●] [Table]
    - Filter button: "Filter" with funnel icon (opens a filter side panel)

Below the title row, a context strip (only visible when "All jobs" is 
selected):
  Light teal background, small icon, low emphasis:
  ℹ "Showing candidates across all 8 active jobs. AI match scores 
  are job-specific — comparing across jobs may be misleading."
  Right side: small "Switch to per-job view ↗" link (also a hint).

When a specific job is selected (e.g., "Senior Frontend Engineer"):
  Context strip changes:
  Job title and meta: "Senior Frontend Engineer · Engineering · 12 
  candidates in pipeline · Hiring team: Layla, Khalid, Sara"
  Right side: "View job details ↗" link

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

VIEW 1 — KANBAN VIEW (default, render this prominently)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

A horizontal scrolling row of stage columns. Each column represents a 
stage and contains candidate cards.

──── STAGE COLUMN STRUCTURE ────

Each column has:
  
  Column header (sticky at top of column):
    - Status dot (small colored circle indicating stage type — purple 
      for active, gray for terminal)
    - Stage name (e.g., "Applied", "Screening", "Assessment", "AI Interview")
    - Count of candidates in stage (e.g., "3")
    - "+" icon on hover/active (to manually add a candidate to this stage)
    - When the stage has special signals, show small indicators:
      "● 2 ready to advance" (small purple text)
      "⚠ 1 stuck" (small amber text)
  
  Column body:
    Scrollable list of candidate cards (stack vertically)
    Empty state when stage has 0 candidates: 
      Centered placeholder: "No candidates yet" (small gray text)
      with subtle "Drop candidates here" affordance on drag hover

──── STAGES TO RENDER ────

Use the canonical "All jobs" view stages:
  1. Applied (5 candidates)
  2. Screening (4 candidates)  
  3. Assessment (3 candidates)
  4. AI Interview (2 candidates) 
  5. HR Interview (2 candidates)
  6. Final Interview (1 candidate)
  7. Offer (1 candidate)
  8. Hired (terminal — show with green tint)
  9. Rejected (terminal — show with gray tint, collapsed by default 
     with "12 rejected this month — click to expand")

──── CANDIDATE CARD DESIGN ────

Each card is a white rounded rectangle (~280px wide), with the 
following layout:

  Top row:
    - Avatar circle (40px, initials with colored background — purple, 
      teal, amber, blue, etc., randomized per candidate)
    - Name (weight 500, truncated if long)
    - AI match pill in the top-right corner:
      Strong (85+): light teal bg, deep teal text (e.g., "✦ 94%")
      Good (70-84): light purple bg, deep purple text (e.g., "✦ 82%")
      Possible (50-69): light amber bg, deep amber text (e.g., "✦ 65%")
      Weak (&lt;50): light gray bg, gray text (e.g., "✦ 42%")
  
  Sub-line under name (small, 11px, gray):
    "Group PM · Noon" (their current role · current company)
  
  Job badge (only in "All jobs" view — small, distinct):
    Below the sub-line, a small pill: "Senior PM" (purple-tinted)
    On click: filters pipeline to that job only
  
  Signal row (when applicable):
    Inline chips showing signal scores for stages already passed:
    - Pre-screen: "✓ Pre-screen 8.5" (light gray pill with checkmark)
    - Assessment: "✓ Assessments 88%" (light purple pill)
    - AI Interview: "✓ AI Interview 89%" (light teal pill)
    Only show signals relevant to candidate's progress.
  
  Bottom row (subtle, low-emphasis):
    Left: "⏱ 4d" (days in stage — turns amber after 5 days, red after 10)
    Right: Small action affordances visible on card hover:
      - Eye icon: View profile
      - Arrow-right icon: Move to next stage  
      - Three-dot kebab: more actions

──── CARD STATES ────

Default: white card, subtle shadow
Hover: slight elevation, action icons appear on the right
Selected (multi-select mode): checkbox visible at top-left, purple ring 
around card
Dragging: card lifts and follows cursor with shadow
Drop target: column briefly highlights when dragged-over

──── EXAMPLE CARDS TO RENDER ────

In "Applied" column (5 cards):

  2. Hassan Al-Najjar — Data Analyst · stc — 80% (Good) — 2d

  4. Faisal Al-Otaibi — Backend Engineer · Aramco — 65% (Possible) — 3d
  5. Rana Aboud — Marketing Manager · Hala — 45% (Weak) — 5d

  4. Reem Al-Shehri — Data Scientist · STC — 71% (Good) — 6d ⚠ (stuck)

In "Assessment" column (3 cards):
  1. Sara Al-Mutairi — Senior PM · Jahez — 90% (Strong) — 9d 
     [Signal: ✓ Assessments 88%]
  2. Maryam Al-Balushi — Frontend Engineer · Tabby — 86% (Strong) — 5d
     [Signal: ✓ Assessments 83%]
  3. Bandar Al-Harbi — Data Analyst · Mrsool — 73% (Good) — 7d
     [Signal: ⏱ Assessment pending] (gray, with "Send reminder" action)

     [Signal: ✓ AI Interview Score 89%]

     [Signal: ✓ AI Interview 87% · ✓ Assessment 92%]

     [Signal: ✓ All previous stages]

     [Signal: "📄 Offer extended yesterday"]

Hired column (terminal):
  Green-tinted, with light celebration treatment.
  Show 1 recent hire as a small card with smaller dimensions:
  "Mariam Al-Otaibi — hired June 1 — Senior Frontend Engineer"

Rejected column (terminal, collapsed by default):
  Gray-tinted, narrower (compressed to ~80px wide).
  Header shows "12 rejected" with an expand arrow.
  When expanded: shows compressed cards with name + reason chip.

──── HORIZONTAL SCROLL BEHAVIOR ────

Columns are wide enough that not all fit on screen — horizontal scroll 
is expected. A small scroll hint at the bottom (gray bar) indicates 
how much more is below the fold.

VIEW 2 — TABLE VIEW (toggle in header)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

When the user clicks "Table" in the view toggle, the pipeline switches

    Job

    Last activity

  ☐ ⬮(avatar) Lina Haddad      Senior PM        Applied        82% Good    —           1d ago    1d        ⋯

                Senior PM · Jahez
  ...

Row hover state: light gray background.
Selected rows: purple background tint, checkbox filled.

Bottom of table: pagination controls if needed ("Showing 1-25 of 47").

──── TABLE FEATURES ────

- Click column header to sort (AI Match defaults to descending sort)
- Sortable columns: Candidate (alpha), Job, Stage, AI Match, Days in stage, Last activity
- Click any row to navigate to candidate profile
- Density toggle: [Comfortable] [Compact] (changes row height)
- Column visibility customization: gear icon at end of header lets user 
  hide/show columns

FILTER SIDE PANEL (triggered by "Filter" button)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Slides in from the right (~360px wide). Doesn't block the pipeline — 
the user can see live results as they adjust filters.

Panel header:
  "Filter pipeline" + count of active filters (e.g., "3 active")
  Right: "Clear all" link + close X

Panel body, scrollable sections:

  ──── QUICK FILTERS (top, prominent) ────
  Pre-built filter buttons (clickable chips):
    [✦ Strong matches only (85+)]
    [⚠ Stuck &gt; 5 days]
    [📋 Missing assessment]
    [🎙 Missing screening call]
    [✓ Recently active (last 24h)]
    [📅 Applied this week]
    [🔄 Recently advanced]
  
  Active quick filter shown with purple background, white text.
  Multiple can be combined.

  ──── BY JOB ────
  Multi-select checkboxes:
    ☐ Senior Product Manager (12)
    ☐ Senior Frontend Engineer (8)
    ☐ Data Scientist (5)
    ☐ Financial Analyst (4)

    [Show more...]

    ☐ Applied (5)

CANDIDATE CARD HOVER STATE &amp; ACTIONS

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

When the user hovers over a candidate card in Kanban view, three 
quick-action icons appear in the bottom-right of the card:

  Eye icon: "View profile" — navigates to candidate profile
  Arrow-right icon: "Move to next stage" — triggers single-step advance
  Three-dot kebab: Opens action menu with:
    - View profile
    - Move to specific stage...
    - Send email
    - Schedule interview
    - Send assessment
    - Add note
    - Add tag
    - View other applications (if candidate has more)
    - Reject with feedback

STAGE COLUMN HEADER ACTIONS

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

When user hovers over a stage column header, three small actions appear:
  + (Add candidate manually to this stage)
  Settings gear (edit stage settings — only for users with permission)
  Kebab (more options: move all visible, archive all, etc.)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

SAVED VIEWS / PRESETS (small but powerful feature)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Below the page header title, a horizontal strip of saved-view tabs:
  
  [All candidates] [Strong matches only] [My active queue] 
  [Stuck candidates] [+ Save current view]
  
  Active tab: purple underline.
  
  Each tab is a saved combination of: job filter + stage filter + 
  other filter criteria. User can save the current filter set as a 
  named view.

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

INTERACTION
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

- Drag and drop candidate cards between columns (Kanban view)
- Cards in Kanban can be moved by drag, or via kebab menu, or via 
  arrow-right quick action
- Clicking a card navigates to candidate profile (preserves return-
  to-pipeline state)
- Multi-select via checkbox (appears on hover in Kanban, always in Table)
- Bulk action bar appears when 1+ candidate selected
- Search filters the visible candidates in real-time
- Filter side panel applies cumulatively with search and saved views
- View toggle (Kanban/Table) preserves selections and filters
- Stuck candidates (&gt;5 days in stage) get an amber indicator on the card
- Empty stages show "No candidates yet" + drop affordance

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

EMPTY STATES (describe; render at least one)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

When pipeline has 0 candidates (e.g., new job, no applications):
  Centered, soft illustration + "No candidates yet"
  Sub-text: "Candidates will appear here when they apply or are added."
  Buttons: [+ Add candidates] [Share apply link] [View job posting]

When filter returns 0 results:
  "No candidates match your filters"
  [Clear filters] [Adjust filters]

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

RESPONSIVE &amp; MOBILE

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

On smaller screens (tablet):
  Kanban columns stack two-up
  Table view becomes the recommended view
  Mobile (phone-sized): Table-only view, simplified

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

DO NOT

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

- Do NOT redesign sidebar/top bar/colors
- Do NOT remove the existing card visual language — refine, don't replace
- Do NOT make AI match scores the only sort option — recruiters use 
  many sorts
- Do NOT show the bulk action bar by default — only when selected
- Do NOT use emoji as primary icons — use lucide-react throughout
- Do NOT make drag-and-drop the ONLY way to move candidates — keyboard 
  and click alternatives required
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults

The pipeline is the recruiter's home base. Every other surface in the 
product is reached from here. Speed, scannability, and confident bulk 
operations are what make this screen great.
</pasted_text>

The refined **Pipeline** is built and verified. Key additions on top of the existing Kanban:

AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This is a REVISION to an existing 
design — apply progressive disclosure to reduce visual density while 
keeping all information accessible. Do not redesign the visual language.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell, primary "+ Create" button
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI-related badges

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

away. Recruiters who want depth get it instantly. Recruiters who just 
want to triage aren't overwhelmed.

PRIMARY action affordance on this page. They're more prominent than 
any other button because they represent the 80% case — the recruiter 
has reviewed the summary and is ready to decide.

  - Opens a confirmation modal: "Move Ahmed to Technical Interview?"
  - Optionally pre-fills an email template invitation
  - On confirm: candidate moves, profile updates, user returned to 
    pipeline OR stays on profile (user preference)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
INTERACTION
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- "Show full summary ↓" expands the AI summary card inline
- "Show 3 more criteria ↓" expands the rubric breakdown inline
- "Show all details" expands the hidden sections inline
- Each expandable section has a "Collapse" affordance once expanded
- Recommended action chips trigger confirmation modals
- Signal timeline rows navigate to relevant tabs
- All cards have hover state (subtle border darkening)
- User's "expanded/collapsed" preferences are remembered per session 
  (so a power user who always expands everything doesn't have to 
  re-expand every time)

  Estimated visual content: ~35% of original

- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (583 lines)">
Design the SCREENING AGENT SETUP WIZARD for "Connect AI", an existing 
AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This wizard REPLACES the previous 
5-tab Configuration screen with a guided step-by-step flow. It's used 
when a recruiter creates a new AI screening agent.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI-related badges
- Typography: clean sans-serif
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke (use lucide-react)
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SIDEBAR NAVIGATION (Screening Calls active)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN: Dashboard
HIRING: Jobs (8), Pipeline (64), Assessments, Video Interviews, 
        Screening Calls ← ACTIVE, Offers (5)
ADMIN: Users (47), Roles, Workflows, Email Templates

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN PHILOSOPHY — ONE THING AT A TIME
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The previous configuration screen showed everything at once and 
recruiters got lost. This wizard fixes that by:

1. Showing ONE step at a time — no parallel tabs, no nested sections
2. Sensible defaults pre-filled — recruiter approves or edits
3. AI-suggested content from the linked job — drafted, not blank
4. Clear progress — recruiter always knows where they are and what's left
5. Each step has one primary purpose — not 5 sub-sections

The wizard is for CREATION. Editing existing agents happens on a 
separate Settings page (different design, not in this prompt).

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WIZARD CHROME (visible on every step)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Breadcrumb: "Screening Calls › New agent"

Top header strip (white card, sticky):
  Left:
    - Title "New screening agent" (16px, weight 500)
    - Below: agent name preview "Engineering Senior Screen" 
      (gray, becomes editable in Step 1)
  Right:
    - "Save and exit" ghost link (saves draft, returns to library)
    - "Discard" ghost link (red text, confirmation modal)

Horizontal step indicator (sticky below header):
  6 pills, connected by thin lines.
  
  Pill states:
    Completed (purple filled circle + checkmark)
    Active (purple outlined circle + number, deeper text)
    Pending (gray circle + number, lighter text)
  
  Step labels:
    1. Basics  →  2. What to ask  →  3. What to say  →  
    4. How it sounds  →  5. How it scores  →  6. Review &amp; launch
  
  Completed steps clickable (returns to that step).
  Pending steps not clickable.

Below the indicator: small "Auto-saved · just now" gray text on the right.

Main content area: white card, generous padding, max-width ~880px, 
centered.

Footer strip (sticky bottom, full-width):
  Left: "← Back" ghost button (disabled on Step 1)
  Right: "Next →" primary purple button
  On Step 6: "Save as draft" ghost + "Launch agent" primary purple
  
  Right side also shows step context: "Step 2 of 6 · ~3 min remaining"

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 1 — BASICS
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Page heading: "Let's set up your screening agent"
Sub-heading: "A few basics to get started. You can change everything 
later."

Single-column form. White card, padded.

Field — Agent name (required):
  Text input
  Placeholder: "e.g. Engineering Senior Screen"
  Helper: "Use a name your team will recognize."

Field — Category (required):
  Dropdown with 4 options:
    - Technical
    - Functional
    - Behavioral  
    - Generic
  Helper: "We'll suggest different defaults based on category."

Field — Languages (required):
  Segmented toggle:
    [English only ●] [Arabic only] [English and Arabic]
  Helper: "Candidates will choose which language to take the call in."

Field — Link this agent to a job (optional):
  
  Two-option radio:
    ● Link to a specific job now
      When selected, reveal:
      Job picker (searchable dropdown):
        "Select a job…"
        - Senior Frontend Engineer · Engineering · Open
        - Engineering Manager · Engineering · Open
        - Data Scientist · Data · Open
        - Senior Product Manager · Product · Open
      
      Below picker: small teal helper:
      ✦ "We'll use this job's JD, rubric, skills, and salary range 
      to draft the agent for you. You can review and edit each step."
    
    ○ Save to library — link to jobs later
      Helper: "Build a generic agent template. Link it to jobs from 
      the library after."

Field — Start from (required, radio group with cards):
  
  Three large radio cards in a row:
  
    ○ ✦ Draft from the linked job (recommended)
      "AI generates a draft agent based on the job's JD, rubric, and 
      salary range. You review each step."
      Sparkle icon, teal accent
      Only available if a job was linked above
      Selected by default if a job was linked
    
    ○ 📋 Start from a starter template
      "Pick from Connect AI's starter library and customize."
      When selected: dropdown appears listing starter templates 
      (Senior Engineering Screen, Mid-Level Engineering, Sales Screen, 
      Customer Service, Generic Knockout, Internal Mobility)
    
    ○ ✏ Start from blank
      "Configure every step from scratch."

Validation:
  - Name, Category, Languages required
  - Start from required
  - "Next" disabled until all required fields filled

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 2 — WHAT TO ASK
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Page heading: "What should the AI screen for?"
Sub-heading: "Define the goals. The AI adapts the conversation to 
cover them, asking follow-ups as needed."

Teal banner at top (only if "Draft from the linked job" was chosen 
in Step 1):
  ✦ "AI drafted these from the Senior Frontend Engineer job. Review 
  and edit before continuing."
  Right: "Regenerate from job" small link

──── PRIMARY SECTION — SCREENING GOALS ────

This step has THREE goal types, but they're presented as ONE prioritized 
list with type pills, not as 3 separate sub-sections. This is the 
biggest change from the old design — no more parallel sub-sections.

A single list of all goals, each with its own card:

  Goal card 1 (Knockout type):
    Top row:
      Type pill: "Knockout" (red, small)
      Drag handle (small dots)
      Goal title: "Work authorization for KSA"
      Right: edit pencil + delete icon
    
    Body (compact, two lines):
      Question: "Are you currently authorized to work in Saudi Arabia 
      without sponsorship?"
      On fail: dropdown "Flag for recruiter review" (Flag / End call early)
  
  Goal card 2 (Knockout type):
    Type pill: "Knockout"
    Goal title: "Salary expectation alignment"
    Question: "What's your salary expectation in SAR per month?"
    Acceptable range: 18,000 – 35,000
    On out-of-range: "Flag for recruiter review"
  
  Goal card 3 (Skill type):
    Type pill: "Skill" (purple, small)
    Drag handle
    Goal title: "React expertise depth"
    
    Body:
      AI guidance: "Ask the candidate to describe a complex React 
      component they built. Probe on state management, performance 
      optimization, and trade-offs."
      Target signal: "Can articulate trade-offs, not just patterns"
      Linked to rubric: [React (must)] (small purple pill, clickable)
  
  Goal card 4 (Skill type):
    Type pill: "Skill"
    Title: "Leadership experience"
    AI guidance: "Ask about team size and direct mentoring. Probe on 
    feedback style, biggest team challenge."
    Target signal: "Has actually led, not just been senior"
    Linked to rubric: [Leadership (must)]
  
  Goal card 5 (Standard type):
    Type pill: "Standard" (gray, small)
    Title: "Closing questions"
    Body: "AI will ask: 'Any questions about the role I can help 
    answer?' and 'When could you start if hired?' and 'Anything else 
    we should know?'"
    Toggle: "Include in this screen" [ON]

At the bottom of the list, three "+ Add goal" buttons, one per type:
  [+ Add knockout goal] (red text)
  [+ Add skill goal] (purple text)
  [+ Add standard goal] (gray text)

Below the goals list, a compact summary strip:
  "Expected call duration: ~14 minutes · 5 goals · 2 knockouts · 
  2 skill probes · 1 standard"

──── SIMPLE EDIT FLOW ────

When user clicks the edit pencil on a goal card, the card EXPANDS in 
place to show all fields editable. No modal, no separate edit page. 
"Save" collapses the card back.

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 3 — WHAT TO SAY
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Page heading: "What can the AI tell candidates?"
Sub-heading: "When candidates ask questions, the AI answers from this 
knowledge base. It never makes up information."

Teal banner at top (only if drafted from job):
  ✦ "AI populated this knowledge base from the job's JD and salary 
  band. Review and add anything specific."

Critical warning banner (light amber, smaller):
  ⚠ "Anything not in this knowledge base, the AI responds: 'Let me 
  note that for your recruiter.' Be specific."

──── KNOWLEDGE BASE — ONE FLAT LIST, NOT 6 ACCORDIONS ────

Big change from the old design: instead of 6 accordion sections 
(About this role, Compensation, Working environment, Hiring process, 
About company, FAQs), it's ONE clean list of knowledge entries with 
a type filter.

Filter bar at top:
  [All types] [Role] [Compensation] [Process] [Company] [Other]
  (small pills, click to filter)

Search input: "Search entries..."

List of knowledge base entries (each a single card):

  Entry 1:
    Type pill: "Role" (purple, small)
    Title: "Day-to-day responsibilities"
    Body (2-3 lines, truncated): "You'll lead frontend development of 
    our customer dashboard. Build new features, mentor 2 junior 
    engineers, contribute to architecture decisions..."
    "Edit" pencil icon on hover
  
  Entry 2:
    Type pill: "Role"
    Title: "Tech stack"
    Body: "React, TypeScript, Next.js, Tailwind, GraphQL, Node.js, 
    PostgreSQL, AWS"
  
  Entry 3:
    Type pill: "Compensation" (amber, small)
    Title: "Salary range to disclose"
    Body: "SAR 22,000 – 28,000 per month, depending on experience"
    Small lock icon next to title: "Sensitive — AI cites exactly"
    Toggle inline: "Disclose to candidates if asked" [ON]
  
  Entry 4:
    Type pill: "Compensation"
    Title: "Vacation and benefits"
    Body: "25 days paid vacation, health insurance, learning budget 
    of SAR 5,000/year"
  
  Entry 5:
    Type pill: "Process" (teal, small)
    Title: "Hiring process"
    Body: "After this screen: technical interview with 2 engineers 
    (60 min), final interview with hiring manager, then offer. 
    Whole process takes 2-3 weeks."
  
  Entry 6:
    Type pill: "Process"
    Title: "Office and remote policy"
    Body: "Hybrid — 3 days in Riyadh office, 2 days remote. Full 
    remote for first 2 weeks of onboarding."

At the bottom of the list: "+ Add knowledge entry" link
  When clicked, an inline form appears at the bottom of the list:
    Type (dropdown), Title (text), Body (textarea), Save/Cancel

──── FALLBACK BEHAVIOR (compact card at bottom) ────
Header: "What the AI says when it doesn't know"
Body (editable textarea, pre-filled):
  "That's a good question. Let me note that for [Recruiter Name] to 
  confirm with you after this call. Is there anything else you'd 
  like to ask?"
Toggle: "Email recruiter with unanswered questions after the call" [ON]

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 4 — HOW IT SOUNDS
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Page heading: "How should the AI sound?"
Sub-heading: "Pick a voice and conversation style. You can preview 
before saving."

Two main sections:

──── SECTION A — VOICE ────

Heading: "Voice"

Grid of voice cards (2 columns):
  
  Card 1: Sarah (English) — Selected
    Avatar/visualization circle
    Voice characteristics: "Warm · Professional · Female · 
    English (American)"
    Play preview button (small triangle icon)
    Selected indicator: purple ring
  
  Card 2: James (English)
    Voice characteristics: "Calm · Direct · Male · English (British)"
    Play preview button
  
  Card 3: Layla (Arabic)
    Voice characteristics: "Warm · Professional · Female · 
    Arabic (Gulf)"
    Play preview button
  
  Card 4: Omar (Arabic)
    Voice characteristics: "Calm · Direct · Male · Arabic (Levantine)"
    Play preview button

If "English and Arabic" was chosen in Step 1, allow selection of TWO 
voices (one per language). Otherwise one voice.

──── SECTION B — CONVERSATION STYLE ────

Heading: "Conversation style"

Three sliders/segmented controls:

  Tone:
    [Formal] [Professional ●] [Friendly] [Casual]
  
  Pace:
    [Fast] [Natural ●] [Patient]
  
  Length target:
    [~10 min] [~15 min ●] [~20 min]
    Helper: "Hard cap at 25 minutes regardless of setting."

──── PREVIEW SECTION (at bottom of step) ────

White card with teal accent left border:
  Header: ✦ "Preview the agent"
  Body:
    Mini transcript showing the AI's opening and one question, using 
    the selected voice and style:
    
    "Hi Ahmed, thanks for taking the time today. I'm Sarah, an AI 
    screening agent for Connect AI. We'll spend about 15 minutes 
    talking through your background. Before we begin — are you ready?"
    
    Play button: "▶ Hear how this sounds (24 seconds)"
    
    Right: "Regenerate preview" link

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 5 — HOW IT SCORES
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Page heading: "How is the evaluation scored?"
Sub-heading: "After the call, the AI evaluates the conversation and 
gives a draft score. You always have the final say."

Teal banner (if drafted from job):
  ✦ "Scoring criteria pulled from the job's rubric. You can adjust 
  weights below."

──── SECTION A — RUBRIC CRITERIA ────

Heading: "What the AI scores"
Sub-header: "Each criterion comes from the linked job's rubric. The 
AI matches conversation content to criteria."

Compact list of criteria, each as a row:
  
  React expertise        must  weight 25%  [slider]
  TypeScript             must  weight 20%  [slider]
  Leadership             must  weight 20%  [slider]
  Communication          must  weight 15%  [slider]
  Cultural fit           nice  weight 10%  [slider]
  Fintech motivation     nice  weight 10%  [slider]
  ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  Total                              100%

Sliders auto-rebalance to 100%. "Reset to job defaults" link below.

──── SECTION B — RECOMMENDATION LOGIC ────

Heading: "AI recommendation"
Sub-header: "The AI gives a recommendation after each call. You decide."

Three settings as toggle rows:

  Generate AI recommendation: [ON, locked]
    Helper: "The AI will suggest 'Advance' or 'Reject' based on scores."
  
  Auto-advance high-confidence candidates: [OFF, with warning if turned ON]
    When toggled ON, shows warning: "⚠ Auto-advance bypasses recruiter 
    review. Most teams keep this OFF. Are you sure?"
    Slider appears: confidence threshold for auto-advance (default 95%)
  
  Auto-reject low-confidence candidates: [OFF, with warning if turned ON]
    Same warning, same slider pattern.

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
STEP 6 — REVIEW &amp; LAUNCH
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Page heading: "Ready to launch?"
Sub-heading: "Review everything before going live. You can edit any 
section after launch."

Single-column summary, each step shown as a clickable card:

Card 1 — Basics:
  Header: "1. Basics" + "Edit" link (jumps to Step 1)
  Compact key-value view:
    Agent name: Engineering Senior Screen
    Category: Technical
    Languages: English and Arabic
    Linked to: Senior Frontend Engineer
    Started from: AI draft

Card 2 — What it asks:
  Header: "2. What to ask" + "Edit"
  Compact summary:
    5 goals total: 2 knockouts · 2 skill probes · 1 standard set
    Top goal: React expertise depth
    Estimated duration: 14 minutes

Card 3 — What it says:
  Header: "3. What to say" + "Edit"
  6 knowledge entries: 2 role · 2 compensation · 2 process
  Salary disclosure: ON

Card 4 — How it sounds:
  Header: "4. How it sounds" + "Edit"
  Voice: Sarah (English) + Layla (Arabic)
  Style: Professional · Natural pace · ~15 min target

Card 5 — How it scores:
  Header: "5. How it scores" + "Edit"
  6 criteria from job rubric
  Auto-advance: OFF · Auto-reject: OFF

──── COMPLIANCE &amp; CONSENT (sticky, prominent — last review item) ────

White card with teal-accent left border (more emphasis than other cards):

  Header: "Compliance &amp; consent"
  
  Pre-filled candidate consent text (read-only here, editable on edit):
    "This call will be conducted by an AI agent. The conversation will 
    be recorded, transcribed, and analyzed to evaluate your fit for 
    this role. The recording and transcript will be kept for 90 days 
    and reviewed by our recruiting team. You can stop the call at any 
    time. By continuing, you consent to this process."
  
  Compliance setting summary (compact, three rows):
    ✓ Content analysis only (no behavioral inference) — locked
    ✓ Human always decides (no auto-reject) — confirmed
    ✓ Right to challenge available — ON
  
  Region rules:
    "Stricter rules apply for: EU, NYC, Illinois (auto-detected by 
    candidate location)"
  
  Right of card: "Customize consent text" small link

──── LAUNCH ACTION (sticky bottom) ────

Final action panel (sticky white card with subtle border):
  Left: Status selector
    ● Launch immediately
    ○ Save as draft (launch later)
  
  Right side:
    "Save as draft" ghost button
    "Launch agent" primary purple button

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
LAUNCH SUCCESS SCREEN
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
After clicking "Launch agent", transition to a celebration screen 
(replaces wizard chrome):

Centered card layout (max-width ~640px):

Large success indicator at top:
  Checkmark in soft green circle
  Heading: "Your screening agent is live"
  Subtitle: "Engineering Senior Screen is ready to take calls."

Linked job card (prominent):
  Heading: "Linked to: Senior Frontend Engineer"
  Body: "When candidates reach the Screening Call stage of this job, 
  the agent will invite them automatically."
  Right: "View job →" link

Quick actions grid (2x2):
  [👁 Preview a call yourself]
  [📋 View in library]
  [🔗 Link to another job]
  [⚙ Edit settings]

If candidates are already waiting in the Screening Call stage for the 
linked job, show a small notice:
  ℹ "3 candidates are currently waiting in the Screening Call stage. 
  They'll receive invitations within 1 hour. [View pipeline →]"

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
INTERACTION
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Step pills clickable for completed steps
- "Save and exit" preserves draft, returns to Library
- AI banners show brief loading on "Regenerate from job"
- Goal cards expand inline for editing
- Knowledge base "+ Add entry" reveals inline form
- Voice preview play button plays a short audio sample
- Sliders update visually
- Toggles with warnings show confirmation banner when turned ON
- "Edit" links on Review step jump back to that step
- Validation is per-step; Next button disabled until step is valid
- Auto-save indicator: "Saving..." then "Auto-saved · just now"

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DO NOT
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT use tabs anywhere in this wizard — strictly linear
- Do NOT show all steps' content at once — only the active step
- Do NOT make the compliance step optional or hidden
- Do NOT enable behavioral analysis options — they remain locked off
- Do NOT use emoji as primary icons — use lucide-react (small emoji 
  in pill labels OK)
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults
- Do NOT default the auto-advance or auto-reject toggles to ON

The wizard is the highest-leverage simplification you can make for 
this feature. The recruiter walks through one decision at a time, 
sees AI-suggested defaults, and reaches "launch" feeling like they 
understand what they built.
</pasted_text>

The **Screening Agent Setup Wizard** is built and verified — a strictly linear 6-step replacement for the old 5-tab config, used for creation (the library's "New screening agent" flows now route into it):

1. **Basics** — name, category, languages, job-link choice, and start-from (AI draft / starter / blank).
2. **What to ask** — one prioritized goal list (Knockout / Skill / Standard pills, inline edit, AI-draft banner, duration summary).
3. **What to say** — a single flat knowledge-base list with type filters + inline add, salary lock/disclose, and fallback behaviour.
4. **How it sounds** — voice cards per language + tone/pace/length, with an audio preview card.
5. **How it scores** — rubric weight sliders (auto-total) and recommendation toggles with auto-advance/auto-reject **off by default** and warnings when enabled.
6. **Review & launch** — per-step summary cards with Edit jumps, a prominent compliance & consent card, then a success screen (linked job, quick actions, waiting-candidates notice).

Wizard chrome throughout: breadcrumb, save/discard, clickable step indicator, auto-saved hint, and a sticky Back/Next footer with step context.

## User

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (467 lines)">
Design the SCREENING AGENT SETTINGS PAGE for "Connect AI", an existing 
AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This page is for EDITING an 
existing agent — different from the wizard (which is for creation).

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI-related badges
- Typography: clean sans-serif
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke (use lucide-react)
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SIDEBAR NAVIGATION (Screening Calls active)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN: Dashboard
HIRING: Jobs (8), Pipeline (64), Assessments, Video Interviews, 
        Screening Calls ← ACTIVE, Offers (5)
ADMIN: Users (47), Roles, Workflows, Email Templates

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN PHILOSOPHY — SETTINGS, NOT WIZARD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The wizard guides linear creation. Settings is for refinement: random 
access, scan-and-edit, see what's set without changing it.

Principles:
1. ONE page, no tabs — everything visible, grouped by purpose
2. Each section is collapsed by default with a one-line summary
3. Clicking a section EXPANDS it inline for editing
4. Save is inline per-section (auto-save on blur for low-risk fields)
5. Major changes (like changing voice) require explicit confirmation
6. Live agent indicator at top — recruiter always sees what's running 
   right now

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
PAGE STRUCTURE
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Breadcrumb: "Screening Calls › Engineering Senior Screen"

Top header strip (white card, sticky):
  
  Top row:
    Left:
      - Agent name "Engineering Senior Screen" (16px, weight 500, 
        click to inline-edit)
      - Sub-line: "Technical · EN/AR · Last edited 2 days ago by Layla"
      - Below: status indicator
        ● Live (green) — accepting calls right now
        OR ◐ Paused (amber) — saved but not accepting calls
        OR ○ Draft (gray) — not yet launched
    
    Right:
      - "Preview a call" ghost button (sparkle icon)
      - "Test on myself" ghost button (envelope icon)
      - Status toggle large: "Agent is live" [ON]
        Helper: small text "Candidates can be screened by this agent"
  
  Bottom row (stats strip, compact):
    Calls completed: 47  |  Avg duration: 14m 32s  |  Completion rate: 87%  
    |  Recruiter agreement with AI: 91%  |  Last call: 2 hours ago

──── BELOW HEADER — TWO-COLUMN LAYOUT ────

LEFT COLUMN (75% — the settings sections):
  Stack of collapsible sections (described below)

RIGHT COLUMN (25%, sticky — context panel):
  Compact card showing "Linked jobs" (described below)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
LEFT COLUMN — SETTINGS SECTIONS
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

All sections are collapsed by default with a clear one-line summary 
when collapsed. Click expand chevron to open.

The sections appear in this order (matches wizard order for familiarity):

──── SECTION 1: BASICS (collapsed by default) ────

Collapsed state:
  Icon: ti-info-circle
  Header: "Basics"
  One-line summary: "Engineering Senior Screen · Technical · 
  EN/AR · Linked to 4 jobs"
  Right: chevron expand icon

Expanded state (white card body):
  Field rows, each with edit-in-place pattern:
    
    Agent name              Engineering Senior Screen     [Edit]
    Category                Technical                     [Edit]
    Languages               English and Arabic            [Edit]
    Created                 May 28, 2026 by Layla (read-only)
    Last edited             June 22, 2026 by Layla (read-only)
  
  Bottom: small "Collapse" link to close section.

──── SECTION 2: WHAT IT ASKS (collapsed by default) ────

Collapsed state:
  Icon: ti-help-circle
  Header: "What it asks"
  One-line summary: "5 goals · 2 knockouts · 2 skill probes · 
  1 standard set · ~14 min expected"
  Right: chevron expand icon

Expanded state:
  
  Top action row:
    Filter chips: [All goals] [Knockout] [Skill] [Standard]
    Right: "+ Add goal" dropdown (Knockout / Skill / Standard)
  
  List of goal cards (same compact format as the wizard's Step 2):
  
    Goal 1 (Knockout):
      Type pill: "Knockout" (red, small)
      Title: "Work authorization for KSA"
      One-line preview: "Q: Are you currently authorized to work in 
      Saudi Arabia without sponsorship? · On fail: Flag"
      Right: edit pencil + drag handle + kebab (Edit / Duplicate / Delete)
      
      When edit pencil clicked, card expands inline showing the full 
      editable form (question text, fail behavior, etc.). Save/Cancel 
      buttons at bottom of expanded card.
    
    Goal 2 (Knockout):
      Title: "Salary expectation alignment"
      Preview: "Range: SAR 18,000–35,000 · On out-of-range: Flag"
    
    Goal 3 (Skill):
      Type pill: "Skill" (purple)
      Title: "React expertise depth"
      Preview: "AI probes: complex component, state mgmt, performance · 
      Linked: React (must)"
    
    Goal 4 (Skill):
      Title: "Leadership experience"
      Preview: "AI probes: team size, mentoring, feedback style · 
      Linked: Leadership (must)"
    
    Goal 5 (Standard):
      Type pill: "Standard" (gray)
      Title: "Closing questions"
      Preview: "3 standard questions covered at the end"
      Toggle inline (right side): "Active" [ON]

──── SECTION 3: WHAT IT SAYS (collapsed by default) ────

Collapsed state:
  Icon: ti-message-circle
  Header: "What it says"
  One-line summary: "8 knowledge entries · Salary disclosure: ON · 
  Last updated 2 days ago"
  Right: chevron expand icon

Expanded state:
  
  Top action row:
    Filter chips: [All] [Role] [Compensation] [Process] [Company] [Other]
    Right: search input + "+ Add entry" button
  
  Compact list of knowledge entries (one row each, not a card per entry — 
  more table-like for scannability):
  
    Type pill | Title                          | Last edited
    Role      | Day-to-day responsibilities    | 2 days ago    [Edit]
    Role      | Tech stack                     | 1 week ago    [Edit]
    Comp      | Salary range                   | 3 weeks ago   [Edit] 🔒
    Comp      | Benefits and vacation          | 3 weeks ago   [Edit]
    Process   | Hiring process steps           | 1 week ago    [Edit]
    Process   | Office and remote policy       | 1 month ago   [Edit]
    Company   | About Connect AI               | 2 months ago  [Edit]
    Other     | Common FAQs                    | 2 weeks ago   [Edit]
  
  The 🔒 icon on "Salary range" indicates a sensitive entry where the 
  AI cites exactly.
  
  Each row clickable → expands inline to show body + edit form.
  
  Below the list, a separate card:
  
  Fallback behavior:
    Header: "When the AI doesn't know"
    Display value (read-only by default): "That's a good question. 
    Let me note that for Layla to confirm with you after this call..."
    [Edit] link to modify
    Toggle: "Email recruiter with unanswered questions" [ON]

──── SECTION 4: HOW IT SOUNDS (collapsed by default) ────

Collapsed state:
  Icon: ti-mood-smile
  Header: "How it sounds"
  One-line summary: "Sarah (English) + Layla (Arabic) · Professional · 
  ~15 min target"
  Right: chevron expand icon

Expanded state:
  
  Voice selection:
    Two horizontal cards side by side (one per language since EN+AR):
    
    English voice (Sarah):
      Small avatar circle + name "Sarah"
      Characteristics: "Warm · Professional · Female · American"
      Play preview button
      "Change voice" link → opens voice picker modal

      Small avatar + name "Layla"
      Characteristics: "Warm · Professional · Female · Gulf"
      Play preview button
      "Change voice" link
  
  Conversation style:
    Three rows of segmented controls:
      Tone: [Formal] [Professional ●] [Friendly] [Casual]
      Pace: [Fast] [Natural ●] [Patient]
      Length: [~10 min] [~15 min ●] [~20 min]
  
  Preview button at bottom:
    [✦ Preview opening line] (teal accent)
    Below it (revealed after click): mini transcript with play button.

──── SECTION 5: HOW IT SCORES (collapsed by default) ────

Collapsed state:
  Icon: ti-chart-bar
  Header: "How it scores"
  One-line summary: "6 criteria from job rubric · Auto-advance: OFF · 
  Auto-reject: OFF"
  Right: chevron expand icon

Expanded state:
  
  Rubric criteria sub-section:
    Header: "Scoring criteria"
    Sub-header: "Weights pulled from linked job's rubric. Adjust here 
    to override."
    
    Compact list (matches wizard format):
      React expertise        must    weight 25%   [slider]
      TypeScript             must    weight 20%   [slider]
      Leadership             must    weight 20%   [slider]
      Communication          must    weight 15%   [slider]
      Cultural fit           nice    weight 10%   [slider]
      Fintech motivation     nice    weight 10%   [slider]
      ──────────────────────────────────────────────
      Total                                  100%

  Recommendation logic sub-section:
    Header: "Recommendation behavior"
    
    Toggle rows:
      Generate AI recommendation: [ON, locked]
      Auto-advance high-confidence candidates: [OFF]
        (When toggled ON, shows confirmation warning + threshold slider)
      Auto-reject low-confidence candidates: [OFF]
        (Same pattern)

──── SECTION 6: COMPLIANCE &amp; CONSENT (collapsed by default) ────

  Icon: ti-shield-check
  Header: "Compliance &amp; consent"

  ✓ Right to challenge ON · Region rules: 3 active"
  Right: chevron expand icon

    Header: "Candidate consent text"

    be recorded, transcribed, and analyzed to evaluate your fit for 
    this role. The recording and transcript will be kept for 90 days 
    and reviewed by our recruiting team. You can stop the call at any 
    time. By continuing, you consent to this process."
    
    [Edit consent text] link
  
  Analysis settings sub-section:
    Header: "Analysis level"
    Radio rows (current state shown, alternatives locked):
      ● Content analysis only (what the candidate says)
      ○ Content + speech patterns (locked — disabled, gray)
        Helper: "Not available — EU AI Act and other regulations 
        restrict behavioral inference."
      ○ Content + voice analysis (locked)

      ☑ EU (auto-detected)
      ☑ NYC (auto-detected)
      ☑ Illinois (auto-detected)

    analysis features."

    Toggle: "Log every decision for bias audit" [ON, locked]
    Sub-text: "Required for compliance."
  
  Right to challenge:
    Toggle: "Allow candidates to challenge AI evaluation" [ON]

Below all sections, a thin horizontal rule, then a small section with 
muted styling:

  Heading: "Danger zone" (small, dark red)
  
  Three rows, each compact:
    Pause agent: [Toggle, currently OFF — meaning agent is live]
      When toggled ON: confirms, then pauses (agent stops accepting calls 
      but settings preserved)
    
    Duplicate this agent:
      "Create a copy of this agent's settings as a new draft."
      [Duplicate] button (ghost)
    
    Archive agent:
      "Hide from library and unlink from all jobs. Historical calls 
      preserved."
      [Archive] button (ghost, gray)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
INTERACTION
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Section expansion:
  - Click any section header to expand
  - Multiple sections can be expanded at once
  - Section state persists during the session (user's preferences 
    remembered)
  - "Expand all" / "Collapse all" toggle at top right of the settings 
    area (small text link)

Inline editing:
  - Most fields use click-to-edit pattern (display value → click → 
    input → save on blur/enter)
  - Auto-save on blur for simple text fields with "Saving..." then 
    "Saved" indicators
  - More complex sections (goals, knowledge entries) expand into 
    inline forms with explicit Save/Cancel

Save confirmation:
  - Trivial changes (typo fixes, minor edits): auto-save with toast 
    confirmation
  - Major changes (changing voice, changing rubric weights, toggling 
    auto-advance): confirmation modal with summary of impact
    Example: "Change voice for 3 active jobs? Candidates currently 
    being screened will continue with the current voice. New calls 
    will use Sarah."

Pause behavior:
  - When agent is paused, top of page shows banner:
    ⚠ "This agent is paused. Candidates won't receive screening calls 
    until you resume."
    Right: "Resume agent" link

Live agent warning:
  - If agent is currently live and user attempts a destructive change 
    (archive, change voice while calls are active), modal warns and 
    requires confirmation

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EDGE STATES (describe briefly)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

If agent has NEVER been launched (still in draft):
  Top header shows "Draft" status pill + "Launch this agent" primary 
  button replacing the "Test on myself" button
  Stats strip hidden (no data yet)
  "Linked jobs" card may be empty with "+ Link to a job" CTA

If agent is paused:
  Top banner warning visible
  All sections still editable
  "Resume agent" toggle at top

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DO NOT
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT use tabs — this is a single page with collapsible sections
- Do NOT default-expand all sections — overwhelming
- Do NOT default-collapse Section 1 (Basics) if the agent is in Draft 
  status — they need to see and complete basics first
- Do NOT enable behavioral analysis options — they remain locked off
- Do NOT show the danger zone above other content — it stays at the 
  bottom
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults
- Do NOT use emoji as primary icons — use lucide-react

The Settings page is where the recruiter LIVES with their agent over 
weeks. The wizard handled the heavy lifting of creation. This page is 
for tuning — quick edits, occasional restructures, monitoring impact. 
Scannable first, editable on click.
</pasted_text>

The Screening Agent **Settings** page is built and verified — the editing surface (reached via "Manage settings" / agent cards), distinct from the creation wizard:

- **Sticky header** — inline-editable name, status indicator (Live / Paused / Draft), Preview + Test buttons, live toggle, and a stats strip (calls, avg duration, completion, AI agreement, last call).
- **Six collapsible sections** (collapsed by default with one-line summaries; Basics auto-expands for drafts): Basics, What it asks, What it says, How it sounds, How it scores, Compliance & consent — each scannable then editable on click, with Expand/Collapse all.
- **Sticky right panel** — Linked jobs (4) and Recent calls, each row navigable.
- **Danger zone** at the bottom — pause / duplicate / archive, with confirmation modals (pause, voice-change impact, archive). Paused state shows a top banner; behavioral analysis stays locked off.

Design the SCREENING AGENT LIBRARY for "Connect AI", an existing 
AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This is the entry point for the 
Screening Calls feature — where recruiters browse, create, and manage 
agents. This replaces an earlier library design with a simplified, 
less crowded version.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI-related badges
- Typography: clean sans-serif
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke (use lucide-react)
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

HIRING: Jobs (8), Pipeline (64), Assessments, Video Interviews, 
        Screening Calls ← ACTIVE, Offers (5)
ADMIN: Users (47), Roles, Workflows, Email Templates

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN PHILOSOPHY — SCAN FAST, ACT FAST
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The library is browsed, not studied. Recruiters come here to:
  - See what agents exist
  - Create a new one (single primary action)
  - Click into an existing one to edit
  - See at-a-glance which agents are active and performing well

Principles:
1. ONE primary action: "+ New agent"
2. Two clean sections: Starter templates and Your agents
3. Each card shows ONLY what helps the recruiter decide what to click
4. No nested modals on the library page itself
5. Clicking a card opens the Settings page (for editing) or starts the 
   wizard (for creating from a starter)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SUB-NAVIGATION (shared across Screening Calls feature)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    clicking opens the wizard with that starter pre-selected in Step 1
