  - "+ Create from scratch" dashed card → opens wizard with "Start 
    from blank" pre-selected in Step 1
  - Top-right kebab on custom card → opens action menu without 
    triggering card click

Status indicator colors:
  ● Live = green dot (active, accepting calls)
  ◐ Draft = amber dot (configured but not launched)
  ○ Paused = gray dot (was live, manually paused)
  Archived agents are filtered out by default (visible only when 
  filter dropdown is set to show them)

Filter and search:
  - Search filters BOTH sections in real-time (starters and custom)
  - Type/Language/Status filters combine (AND logic)
  - Active filters shown as removable chips below the filter bar

Kebab actions on custom card:
  - Edit (default, same as clicking card)
  - Duplicate (creates editable copy as a new draft)
  - Pause / Resume (depending on current state)
  - Archive (with confirmation)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT add a dropdown menu to the "+ New agent" button — single 
  action only, opens the wizard
- Do NOT show all the configuration options on this page — the 
  library is for browsing, not editing
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults
- Do NOT use emoji as primary icons — use lucide-react
- Do NOT make starter cards visually identical to custom cards — they 
  serve different purposes and should look distinguishable
- Do NOT include a separate "Manage integrations" view here — that 
  link goes to a separate page

The library is the start of every screening call interaction. Make 
it fast to scan, with one clear primary action ("New agent") and 
obvious paths into existing agents.

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (399 lines)">
Design the RECRUITER REVIEW SURFACE for a completed AI screening call 
in "Connect AI", an existing AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This 
is where the recruiter reviews a candidate's completed screening call, 
sees the AI's evaluation, overrides if needed, and confirms a decision.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EXISTING VISUAL LANGUAGE (match precisely)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Light theme, soft off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards, ~12px rounded corners, very subtle shadow
- LEFT SIDEBAR: section headers in small uppercase gray (MAIN, HIRING, 
  ADMIN). Active items: light lavender background, deep purple text 
  (#6B5BFF), thin purple left-border indicator
- TOP BAR: search with "AI" teal badge, EN/AR language toggle, 
  dark-mode toggle, notification bell
- Primary accent: purple/violet (#6B5BFF)
- Secondary accent: teal/cyan (#5EEAD4) for AI-related badges
- Typography: clean sans-serif
- Icons: outlined, ~1.5px stroke (use lucide-react)
- Product supports English + Arabic (RTL) — render in English

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SIDEBAR NAVIGATION (Pipeline active)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
MAIN: Dashboard
HIRING: Jobs (8), Pipeline (64) ← ACTIVE, Assessments, Video Interviews, 
        Screening Calls, Offers (5)
ADMIN: Users (47), Roles, Workflows, Email Templates

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN PHILOSOPHY — TRUST FAST, DECIDE FAST
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The old Review surface was dense — transcript, AI evaluation, override 
controls, trust signals, follow-ups all visible at once. Recruiters 
got lost.

The redesign sequences the recruiter's actual task into 3 questions, 
in order:

  1. CAN I TRUST THIS CALL?     → Quick integrity check at the top
  2. WHAT DID THE AI FIND?      → Summary + per-goal evaluation
  3. WHAT'S MY DECISION?        → Action panel at the bottom

If the recruiter agrees with the AI, this is a 2-minute decision. If 
they disagree or want depth, the transcript and override controls are 
one click away.

Principles:
1. ONE primary read-path top to bottom — not a parallel 2-column dump
2. Recommended action UP FRONT — recruiter usually agrees with AI
3. Evidence and overrides revealed PROGRESSIVELY — not always visible
4. Transcript is a SEPARATE view, not the main one — recruiters don't 
   read transcripts by default; they read summaries

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
PAGE STRUCTURE
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Breadcrumb: "Pipeline › Senior Frontend Engineer › Ahmed Hassan › 
Screening Call"

Top header strip (white card, sticky):
  Left:
    - Avatar (initials "AH" purple bg, 40px) + name "Ahmed Hassan" 
      (16px, weight 500)
    - Sub-line: "Senior Frontend Engineer · AI Screening Call · 
      Completed June 9, 2026 at 3:42 PM GST"
  Right:
    - "View candidate profile →" ghost link
    - "Re-run AI evaluation" ghost button (sparkle icon, low emphasis)
    - Primary purple button: "Confirm &amp; advance" with dropdown chevron
      Dropdown shows: Confirm &amp; advance / Confirm &amp; reject / 
      Save without decision

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 1 — RECOMMENDED ACTION (the headline)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

A single prominent white card with teal-accent left border (3px), 
generous padding. This is the FIRST thing the recruiter sees after 
the header — it answers their question: "What should I do?"

Card layout:

  Top label (small caps, gray): "✦ AI RECOMMENDATION"
  
  Large recommendation pill/badge (centered, big):
    "● Advance to Technical Interview"
    Color: green if Advance, red if Reject, amber if Mixed/Unclear
    Below pill: "High confidence (4.5/5)"
  
  Below the pill, condensed reasoning (1-2 sentences max):
    "Ahmed showed strong technical depth on React, gave specific 
    leadership examples, and articulated clear motivation for fintech. 
    Salary expectation was vague — recommend confirming with him."
  
  Below the reasoning, action chips in a row:
    [✓ Advance to Technical Interview] (primary purple, with arrow)
    [✕ Reject with feedback] (ghost, gray)
    [⏱ Save for later] (ghost)
  
  Bottom of card: small "Show full reasoning ↓" link
    When clicked: expands inline to show the long-form AI explanation 
    (the detailed paragraph from old Prompt 5).

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 2 — TRUST SIGNALS (compact integrity check)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

A single horizontal strip (not a tall card). Compact, scannable.

Header: "Submission integrity"
Right: small gray "✓ All checks clear"

Six compact indicators in a row, each with icon + label + state:
  ✓ Consent accepted        (14:32 PM GST)
  ✓ Recording quality       (Excellent)
  ✓ Voice identity matched  (Same as application)
  ✓ AI-use not detected     (Natural pauses)
  ✓ No suspicious patterns  (Time + responses normal)
  ✓ All topics covered      (5 of 5)

Each indicator: green check + label.
If any indicator failed/flagged: amber/red instead of green, with 
"View details" link.

Below the strip: small "Show full submission details ↓" link.

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 3 — WHAT THE AI FOUND (per-goal evaluation)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

White card. Header: "Per-goal evaluation"
Sub-header: "How the AI scored against the agent's goals."

A clean list of goals, each as a compact row:

  Goal 1: React expertise depth (must)
    Score: 9 / 10
    Bar: ▰▰▰▰▰▰▰▰▰░
    Evidence (one-line quote, italics): 
      "...virtualization with react-window, combined with memoization 
      on the row components..."
    Right of row: [Jump to 6:24 in transcript →] small link
    Override indicator: 🎯 (gray, becomes purple when recruiter overrides)

  Goal 2: Leadership experience (must)
    Score: 8 / 10
    Bar: ▰▰▰▰▰▰▰▰░░
    Evidence: "I gave Mariam weekly 1-on-1s for six months..."
    [Jump to 10:47 →]

  Goal 3: Fintech motivation (nice)
    Score: 9 / 10
    Bar: ▰▰▰▰▰▰▰▰▰░
    Evidence: "I've been a customer of Saudi neobanks for two years..."
    [Jump to 13:15 →]

──── KNOCKOUT QUESTIONS (sub-section, visually grouped) ────

A horizontal divider with "Knockouts" label.

  Knockout 1: Work authorization
    Status pill: ✓ Confirmed (green)
    Detail: "KSA citizen — no sponsorship needed"
    [Jump to 1:24 →]

  Knockout 2: Salary expectation
    Status pill: ⚠ Unclear (amber)
    Detail: "Candidate said 'around twenty-eight' without specifying 
    currency or range. Needs follow-up."
    [Jump to 14:30 →]
    Right: [+ Add to follow-up email] small link

  Knockout 3: Notice period
    Status pill: ✓ Captured (green)
    Detail: "1 month"

Bottom of card: small text
  "Weighted score: 87/100 · 6 of 6 must-haves met"
  Right: "How is this calculated?" small teal link

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 4 — DEEPER REVIEW (collapsed by default, expandable)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

A single white card with "Show deeper review ↓" expander. When 
collapsed, just shows the heading and a one-line summary.

Collapsed state:
  Header: "Deeper review"
  One-line: "Full transcript · Candidate questions · Audio playback · 
  Override scores"
  Right: chevron expand icon

Expanded state shows three sub-sections inside the card:

──── SUB-SECTION 4A — TRANSCRIPT ────

Compact transcript viewer (not the dominant element it was before):
  
  Top row:
    "Transcript" label + search input ("Search transcript...") + 
    "Download as PDF" small link
  
  Scrollable transcript area (max-height ~400px, with scroll):
    Sample transcript with timestamps + speaker labels:
    
    [0:00] AI: Hi Ahmed, thanks for taking the time today...
    [0:18] Ahmed: Yes, I'm ready.
    [0:21] AI: Great. Let's start with work authorization...
    ... (more entries)
  
  Highlighting:
    - Rubric-matched phrases highlighted in light purple
    - Click any highlighted phrase to see its rubric mapping
  
  Below the transcript: small audio player mock
    Play button + waveform + duration "16:42"
    "Listen to original audio" link

──── SUB-SECTION 4B — CANDIDATE QUESTIONS ────

Two compact lists side by side:

  Left list — "Answered by AI (4)":
    Q: "What's the team size?" 
       AI: "The frontend team is 8 engineers..."
       [Jump to 11:15 →]
    
    Q: "Is the role remote-friendly?"
       AI: "Hybrid — 2 days in office..."
       [Jump to 13:45 →]
    
    Q: "What's the tech stack?"
       AI answered. [Jump →]
    
    Q: "What's the typical career progression?"
       AI answered. [Jump →]
  
  Right list — "Noted for follow-up (2)":
    Q: "Is there a sign-on bonus?"
       Marked for: Layla to follow up
       [+ Add to follow-up email →]
    
    Q: "How much travel is expected?"
       Marked for: Layla to follow up
       [+ Add to follow-up email →]

──── SUB-SECTION 4C — OVERRIDE SCORES ────

Compact override table:
  
  Header: "Adjust scores if you disagree"
  Sub-header: "Your override becomes the final score. Required if you 
  differ by 2+ points on any criterion."
  
  Table rows:
    Goal                       AI score   Your score    
    React expertise            9          [9] (input field, default to AI)
    Leadership                 8          [8]
    Fintech motivation         9          [9]
    Communication              9          [9]
    
  When recruiter changes a score: row highlights, and an "override 
  reason" textarea appears at the bottom (required if difference &gt;2):
    "Why did you change this score?"
    Required textarea.
  
  Below the table:
    Final recommendation override radio:
      ● Use AI recommendation: Advance to Technical Interview
      ○ Override: Reject candidate
      ○ Override: Request another screening
    
    If override radio selected, reveal a textarea: 
      "Reason for override (required)"

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 5 — YOUR FOLLOW-UP (sticky right side, but as a strip)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

A compact white card at the BOTTOM of the main column (not a sticky 
sidebar — keeping the linear top-to-bottom flow).

Header: "Things to follow up on"
Sub-header: "Auto-generated from the call. Edit as needed."

Compact checklist:
  ☐ Confirm exact salary expectation (candidate was vague)
  ☐ Answer: Sign-on bonus availability
  ☐ Answer: Travel expectations for the role
  ☐ Schedule technical interview

Each row hover: shows edit/delete icons.

Right side of card:
  Two buttons:
    [✉ Generate follow-up email] (primary teal, sparkle icon)
    [💬 Discuss with team] (ghost — adds note tagged @hiring-team)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
FOOTER — CONFIRM DECISION (sticky bottom action bar)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

A sticky bar at the bottom of the page (white card, slight shadow), 
always visible.

Left side:
  Status indicator:
    "Your decision: Advance to Technical Interview"
    (Updates if recruiter overrides)
    Small text below: "Matching AI recommendation"
    OR if overridden: "Overriding AI (was: Advance)" with reason 
    summary

Right side:
  Two buttons:
    [Confirm &amp; advance] primary purple (large)
    [Save without deciding] ghost
  
  Sub-text below button: "Saves your evaluation; you can decide later."

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
EDGE STATES (describe; don't render multiple)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

If AI confidence is LOW (e.g., &lt; 3/5):
  Section 1 (Recommended action) card uses amber accent instead of 
  green/red. Text reads: "● Mixed signals — recommend recruiter 
  review"
  Confidence: "Low confidence (2.5/5) — manual review recommended"

If candidate ended call early:
  Section 1 reads: "● Call ended early — incomplete evaluation"
  Section 2 shows ⚠ "Only 3 of 5 topics covered"
  Action chips: [Reschedule] [Reject] [Continue with partial data]

If integrity flags fired:
  Section 2 (Trust signals) shows amber/red indicators
  Section 1 includes a note: "⚠ Submission integrity flagged — review 
  before deciding"

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
INTERACTION
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

- The page reads top-to-bottom: Recommendation → Trust → Evaluation 
  → Deeper review → Follow-up → Confirm
- "Show full reasoning ↓" on Section 1 expands the AI explanation 
  inline
- "Show full submission details ↓" on Section 2 expands trust signals 
  to a verbose list
- "Show deeper review ↓" on Section 4 expands the entire deeper review 
  card (transcript + questions + overrides)
- "Jump to [timestamp] →" links expand Section 4 and scroll the 
  transcript to that moment
- Override scores trigger inline highlighting and required reason 
  textarea
- Sticky footer "Confirm &amp; advance" finalizes the evaluation
- The candidate is moved in the pipeline immediately on confirm

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
COMPARISON TO ORIGINAL REVIEW SURFACE
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Original Review surface default view:
  - Two columns simultaneously (60% left content, 40% right actions)
  - AI evaluation, transcript, override controls all visible at once
  - 5+ major sections competing for attention
  - Estimated visual content: 100%

New Review surface default view:
  - Single column, linear flow
  - 3 main sections visible (Recommendation, Trust, Evaluation)
  - Deeper review (transcript, overrides) collapsed by default
  - Estimated visual content: ~40% of original

All original content remains accessible via "Show deeper review" 
expander. Recruiters who agree with AI get a 2-minute review. 
Recruiters who want depth get it with one click.

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DO NOT
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- Do NOT make the transcript the dominant element — it lives inside 
  the collapsed "Deeper review" section
- Do NOT show override controls by default — they appear when the 
  recruiter expands "Deeper review"
- Do NOT auto-confirm the AI recommendation — recruiter must click 
  "Confirm &amp; advance"
- Do NOT use a 2-column layout — the linear flow is the key UX change
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults
- Do NOT use emoji as primary icons — use lucide-react

The Review surface is where the AI screening feature delivers value. 
A 16-minute call should be reviewable in 2-3 minutes if the recruiter 
agrees. The progressive disclosure (deeper review) is what makes this 
possible without losing access to depth when needed.
</pasted_text>

This redesigns the existing screening review surface into a linear, progressive-disclosure flow. Let me rewrite it.

All sections verified — recommendation headline, trust strip, per-goal evaluation, collapsed deeper review (expands to transcript + questions + overrides), follow-up, and sticky decision footer.

_[tool: snip]_

_[tool: ready_for_verification]_

_[tool: snip]_

The recruiter review surface is redesigned into a single linear, progressive-disclosure flow — verified and shipped:

1. **Recommended action** (headline) — teal-accented card with the big "Advance to Technical Interview" recommendation, confidence, condensed reasoning, action chips, and a "Show full reasoning" expander.
2. **Submission integrity** — a compact horizontal strip of six green checks with "Show full details."
3. **Per-goal evaluation** — scores + bars + one-line evidence quotes with jump-to-timestamp links, a grouped Knockouts sub-section (incl. the ⚠ unclear salary), and the weighted-score footer.
4. **Deeper review** (collapsed by default) — expands to transcript (search, highlights, audio mock), candidate questions (answered / follow-up), and override-score controls with required-reason gating + final recommendation radios.
5. **Follow-up** — auto-generated checklist + Generate email / Discuss with team.
- **Sticky decision footer** — shows your decision (matching or overriding AI) with Confirm & advance / Save without deciding.

Transcript and overrides stay one click away, so an agreeing recruiter reviews in ~2 minutes while depth remains accessible.

## User

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (609 lines)">
Design the CANDIDATE SCREENING CALL EXPERIENCE for "Connect AI", an 
existing AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This is the candidate-
facing side of the AI screening call feature — what the candidate 
sees from invitation through call completion.

This is a CANDIDATE-FACING surface (no admin sidebar, no internal 
user). The candidate received an email and clicked the link. They are 
not logged into a Connect AI account.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
CANDIDATE-FACING CHROME (different from admin app)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- No left sidebar, no admin top bar
- Top: company branding ("Connect AI" logo small, optionally co-branded 
  "for [Hiring Company]")
- Bottom: small footer with "Powered by Connect AI" + privacy + help links
- Visual language matches Connect AI palette but with more generous 
  spacing and calmer tone — this is the candidate's experience
- Light theme, off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards with soft shadows, slightly larger padding than admin views
- Primary purple #6B5BFF, teal accent #5EEAD4
- Render in English (with EN/AR toggle visible everywhere)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN PHILOSOPHY — ONE JOURNEY, MANY STATES
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The old design split the candidate experience into 3 separate screens 
(Pre-Call, In-Call, Post-Call). That made each screen feel disconnected.

The new design treats it as ONE journey with multiple states. The 
candidate moves through:

  1. WELCOME → consent → channel choice → ready check  (pre-call)
  2. LIVE CALL                                          (in-call)
  3. CONFIRMATION → next steps                          (post-call)

Each state has its own UI, but they share the same chrome, same tone, 
same visual language — so the candidate never feels like they've been 
handed off to a different system.

Principles:
1. Always tell the candidate what's happening and what's next
2. Make AI involvement EXPLICIT — never hide that they're talking to AI
3. Consent is prominent, not buried
4. The candidate chooses how to take the call — phone or browser
5. Trust through transparency, not stealth

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WHAT TO BUILD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
A single React artifact with five states the user can navigate through 
(use useState for state management):

State 1: WELCOME &amp; CONSENT
State 2: CHANNEL CHOICE (phone vs browser)
State 3: READY CHECK (mic test for browser; phone confirmation for phone)
State 4: IN-CALL (browser path; phone has no UI)
State 5: POST-CALL CONFIRMATION

Render State 1 as default. Include navigation buttons to transition 
between states so the user can preview each.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SHARED CHROME (visible in all states)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar (60px tall, light):
  Left: "Connect AI" logo (~32px, small)
  Center: empty (or a step indicator in States 2-3)
  Right: 
    - Language toggle: [EN ●] [العربية]
    - Help link (small, gray)

Footer (60px tall, low emphasis):
  Centered text: "Powered by Connect AI · Privacy · Help"

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

STATE 1 — WELCOME &amp; CONSENT

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Main content (centered, max-width 720px):

  Heading (32px, weight 500):
    "Hi Ahmed, your screening call awaits."
  
  Sub-heading (14px, gray):
    "We're excited to talk with you about the Senior Frontend Engineer 
    role at Connect AI."

  ──── Hero card (white, generous padding, teal-accent left border) ────
  
  Top label (small caps, teal, with sparkle icon): 
    "✦ AI-CONDUCTED CALL"
  
  Heading (20px, weight 500):
    "This is an AI screening call"
  
  Body (14px, line-height 1.6):
    "Your initial screen for this role will be conducted by Connect 
    AI's AI agent — not a human recruiter. This is shorter than a 
    traditional phone screen and more flexible: you can take it 
    whenever you're ready, in English or Arabic, on your phone or in 
    your browser.
    
    Your conversation will be recorded, transcribed, and reviewed by 
    our recruiting team. The team makes all hiring decisions — the AI 
    doesn't decide anything alone."
  
  Three small info chips in a row at the bottom of the card:
    [⏱ About 15 minutes]
    [🌐 English or Arabic]
    [📱 Phone or browser]

  ──── Card "What we'll cover" (white) ────
  
  Header: "What we'll talk about"
  
  Compact list (no card per item, just bulleted):
    • Your background and work authorization
    • Your experience with React and TypeScript
    • Your leadership and team experience
    • Your interest in this role
    • Any questions you have for us

  ──── Card "Your consent" (white, teal-accent left border, prominent) ────
  
  Header: "Your consent"
  Sub-header: "Required before starting."
  
  Three checkboxes, each required:
    
    ☐ "I understand this call will be conducted by AI"
    ☐ "I consent to the call being recorded and transcribed for 
       evaluation"
    ☐ "I understand my recording will be stored for 90 days and 
       reviewed by Connect AI's recruiting team"
  
  Below the checkboxes (low emphasis):
    Helper text 1: "Prefer to talk with a human recruiter instead? 
    [Request human screening →]" (small link)
    
    Helper text 2: "Need to challenge the AI's evaluation later? 
    You'll have that option afterwards."

  ──── Bottom action area ────
  
  Primary button: "Choose how to take the call →" 
    (purple, large, full-width on mobile, disabled until all 3 consent 
    boxes checked)
  
  Below: small gray text "Can't take it now? Resume later from your 
  invitation email."

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

STATE 2 — CHANNEL CHOICE

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar adds a step indicator:
  "Step 1 of 2: How would you like to take the call?"

    "How would you like to take the call?"

    "Both options work equally well. Pick whichever is more comfortable."

  ──── Two large choice cards side by side ────

  Card A — "Phone call" (selectable):
    Card container: white, 12px rounded, click-to-select

    Title: "We'll call your phone" (16px, weight 500)

      "Our AI will call you at your phone number. No app needed — just 
      answer when it rings."
    
    Below description, three small benefits:
      ✓ Works on any phone (smartphone or basic)
      ✓ Use your existing phone signal
      ✓ Can take it anywhere
    
    Selection indicator: radio circle at top-right corner
    
    When selected (radio filled, purple ring around card), expand below:
      Phone number input (pre-filled): "+966 50 123 4567"
      Country code dropdown
      Helper: "We'll call from this number: +966 11 XXX XXXX. Save it 
      as 'Connect AI' so you don't miss the call."

  Card B — "Browser call" (selectable, pre-selected by default):
    
    Top: headset icon (lucide ti-headphones, ~48px, teal)
    
    Title: "Take it in your browser"
    
    Description:
      "Talk through your computer or phone's microphone, right here in 
      your browser."
    
    Benefits:
      ✓ Works on any device with a microphone
      ✓ No phone signal needed — uses internet
      ✓ See live captions during the call
    
    Selection indicator: radio circle (filled by default)
    
    When selected, expand:
      Helper: "We'll test your microphone and connection on the next 
      screen."
      Sub-helper (small, gray): "Recommended: a quiet room and 
      headphones for the best experience."

  ──── Bottom action area ────
  
  Two-button row:
    Left: "← Back" (ghost link)
    Right: "Continue →" (primary purple, disabled until a channel selected)

  "Step 2 of 2: Get ready"

──── BROWSER PATH (render this as the default) ────

Main content (centered, max-width 720px):

  Heading (24px, weight 500):
    "Let's make sure everything's set up"
  
  Sub-heading (14px, gray):
    "A quick mic test before we begin."

  ──── Card "Microphone check" (white, generous padding) ────
  
  Centered visual: 
    Large microphone icon (~80px) with an animated waveform mock 
    around it (4-6 vertical bars with random heights, pulsing).
    Below the icon: status text in green
    "✓ Microphone working — say something to test"
    
    Alternative states (describe; don't render):
      If mic blocked: red icon + "Microphone access needed — click to enable"
      If no input detected: amber icon + "We can't hear you — try speaking"
  
  Below the visual, a compact tips card:
    Header: "Tips for the best call"
    Compact bullets:
      • Find a quiet space with minimal background noise
      • Use headphones if you have them
      • Speak clearly and at a normal pace
      • You can ask the AI to repeat anything

  ──── Card "Choose your language" (white) ────

    [English ●] [العربية]

  or 'switch to Arabic'."

    • The AI will introduce itself and confirm you're ready
    • You'll have a natural conversation — feel free to ask questions
    • Call lasts about 15 minutes (max 25)
    • Say "give me a second" if you need a moment to think
    • The AI handles silence — take your time

  ──── Bottom action area ────

    (purple, large, with phone-pickup icon)
  
  Below: ghost link "Save and continue later"

STATE 4 — IN-CALL (browser path; phone has no UI)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar changes (minimal, focused):
  Left: "Connect AI" logo (small)
  Center: Call status: "● Live · 6:23 / ~15:00" (pulsing green dot)
  Right: Language indicator: "EN ▾" (clickable to switch)

Main call area (centered, max-width 760px):

  ──── AI presence visualization (top) ────
  
  Large circular element (~140px diameter):
    A gradient orb or breathing pulse animation (purple/teal gradient, 
    soft, never harsh)
    Represents the AI's "presence" during the conversation
  
  Below the orb (centered):
    Small label: "Connect AI Assistant"
    Small teal pill: "AI Screening Agent"
  
  Status text (gray, italic, small):
    Currently: "✓ Listening — take your time"
    
    Alternative states (describe):
      "Speaking..." (orb pulses with rhythm)
      "Thinking..." (orb shows three small animated dots)
      "Paused" (orb is calm, gray)

  ──── Live transcript / captions card (the main focus of the screen) ────
  
  White card, comfortable padding, max-width 660px.
  
  Style:
    - AI messages: left-aligned, light gray text, small teal sparkle 
      icon prefix
    - Candidate messages: right-aligned, slightly darker text
    - Current speaker's message has a thin animated cursor at the end
  
  Sample (last 4 exchanges):
  
    ✦ AI · 5:42
    "Got it — six years of React experience, with the last three at 
    Acme Fintech. Can you walk me through a particularly complex 
    component you built there?"
    
    Ahmed · 5:54
    "Sure. We had a transaction timeline that showed up to ten thousand 
    transactions per user. The challenge was performance — we were 
    re-rendering the entire list on every state change."
    
    ✦ AI · 6:18
    "Interesting. How did you approach that?"
    
    Ahmed · 6:23 (current, with animated cursor)
    "We used virtualization with react-window, combined with memoization 
    on the row components. We also restructured the state so that filter 
    changes only..."
  
  Scroll-up indicator at top of card: "↑ Show earlier in conversation"

  ──── Side panel / contextual help (right of transcript, narrow ~200px) ────
  
  Sticky white card with three small sub-cards:
  
  Sub-card 1 — "Need help?":
    Compact action buttons:
      [🔁 Ask AI to repeat]
      [⏸ Pause for a moment]
      [🔇 Mute briefly]
      [💬 Ask for clarification]
    
    Small text below: "You can also just say these aloud — 'can you 
    repeat that?' or 'give me a second'."
  
  Sub-card 2 — "Today's screening":
    Progress checklist (small):
      ✓ Background &amp; work authorization
      ✓ React experience (in progress)
      ○ Leadership experience
      ○ Fintech interest
      ○ Your questions for us
    
    Small note at bottom: "About 40% through."

  ──── Bottom control bar (sticky bottom, full width, white card) ────
  
  Left side:
    Microphone state: large mic icon + "Mic on" (green text)
    Click to toggle mute. When muted: red icon + "Muted — AI is waiting"
  
  Center: (intentionally minimal)
    Small toggle: "CC: Captions on" (clickable to hide/show transcript)
  
  Right side:
    Small ghost icon button: settings (gear)
    Red button: "End call" (light red bg, requires confirmation on click)

  ──── Special in-call states (describe; don't render as main) ────
  
  Connection lost overlay:
    Full-screen amber banner:
    "Connection lost — reconnecting..."
    Timer pauses, transcript saved.
    When reconnected: "Reconnected. Picking up where we left off..."
  
  End-of-call transition:
    Status changes to "Wrapping up..."
    AI gives closing summary in transcript
    Smooth transition to State 5

STATE 5 — POST-CALL CONFIRMATION

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar returns to minimal (logo + language toggle).

  ──── Hero success area (top) ────
  
  Centered:
    Large soft green circle with white checkmark (~72px)
    Heading (28px, weight 500): "All done, Ahmed"
    Sub-heading (14px, gray): "Thanks for taking the time to talk 
    with us today."

  ──── Card "Your call summary" (white) ────
  
  Header row:
    Left: "Call completed"
    Right: "June 9, 2026 · 3:42 PM GST" (small gray)
  
  Compact stats grid (2 columns):
    Duration         16 minutes 42 seconds
    Language         English
    Topics covered   5 of 5
    Channel          Browser
  
  Sub-section: "Confirmation ID"
    ID: SCRN-AH-9X4M2 (selectable, monospace)
    Helper: "Save this if you need to reference your call."

  ──── Card "What happens next" (white) ────
  
  Header: "What happens next"
  Numbered list:
    1. Our recruiting team reviews your call within 5 business days
    2. You'll receive an email at ahmed.hassan@email.com with the decision
    3. If you advance, we'll set up your next interview round with our 
       engineering team

  ──── Card "Questions you asked us" (white) ────
  
  Header: "We made note of your questions"
  Sub-header: "Your recruiter will follow up on these in your next email."
  
  List of questions captured:
    • "What's the typical career progression for senior engineers at 
       Connect AI?"
    • "Is there a remote work allowance for equipment?"
  
  Empty state (if no questions asked):
    "You didn't ask any questions during the call. If you think of 
    anything later, reply to your invitation email to reach your 
    recruiter."

  ──── Card "Review your call" (white, teal-accent left border) ────
  
  Header (with sparkle icon): "✦ Want to review what you said?"
  Body:
    "You can review the full transcript. This won't change anything — 
    it's just for your records."
  Button: "View transcript →" (ghost)

  ──── Card "Concerns about the evaluation?" (low emphasis, smaller) ────
  
  Header: "Right to challenge"
  Body:
    "If after receiving our decision you feel the AI's evaluation was 
    unfair or inaccurate, you have the right to request a human review."
  Link: "Learn how →"

  ──── Section "While you wait" (low emphasis) ────
  
  Three small horizontal cards:
    Card 1: 💼 Browse other open roles → careers link
    Card 2: 📚 Learn more about Connect AI → blog link
    Card 3: 💬 Got more questions? → contact link

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

SECONDARY STATE — EARLY ENDED CALL

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

If the candidate clicks "End Call" before completion:

  Heading: "Call ended early"
  Body: "It looks like the call ended before all topics were covered. 
  No problem — here's what to do:"
  
  Numbered options:
    1. Want to finish later? Your call link is valid for 48 more hours.
       [Resume call →] (primary)
    2. Want to schedule with a human instead?
       [Request human screening →]
    3. Want to withdraw your application?
       [Withdraw application] (small, gray)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

INTERACTION

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

State transitions:
  State 1 → State 2: All 3 consent boxes checked + "Choose how" button
  State 2 → State 3: Channel selected + "Continue" button
  State 3 → State 4 (browser): Mic test passing + "I'm ready" button
  State 3 → State 4 (phone): "Confirm and wait" → call begins
  State 4 → State 5: AI ends call naturally OR candidate clicks End Call

In-call interactions:
  - Orb animates based on speaker state (pulsing while AI speaks, calm 
    when listening, dots when thinking)
  - Live transcript scrolls as messages stream in
  - Mute button toggles
  - Captions toggle hides/shows the transcript card
  - "End call" requires confirmation modal: "End the call early? Your 
    responses so far will be saved."
  - Quick action buttons send signals to AI (visual only in artifact)

Language switching:
  - EN/AR toggle updates the entire interface
  - Mid-call language switching available via voice command 
    (transcript shows AI confirming switch)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

DO NOT

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

- Do NOT include any admin chrome (sidebar, top bar)
- Do NOT use phrases that obscure that this is AI ("virtual recruiter", 
  "automated assistant", "smart agent") — always say "AI"
- Do NOT bury consent — it stays in its own prominent card
- Do NOT make "End call" too subtle to find — must be visible during call
- Do NOT add a video feed of any kind — this is voice only
- Do NOT show AI scores or evaluation to the candidate at any point
- Do NOT pretend the AI was a human in the post-call screen
- Do NOT promise specific outcomes ("you'll definitely hear back 
  positively")
- Do NOT use emoji as primary icons (small emoji in info chips and 
  quick action labels acceptable) — use lucide-react throughout
- Do NOT use generic shadcn defaults

The candidate experience must feel calm, fair, and respectful at every 
step. The candidate should never wonder what's happening or what's next. 
Transparency about AI involvement is the foundation of trust — without 
it, recruiters get fewer completions, more complaints, and more legal 
exposure.

This is often a candidate's first deep touch with the company. Every 
detail signals how seriously the company takes their time and their 
rights.
</pasted_text>

## Assistant

_[tool: snip]_

_[tool: eval_js]_

The candidate screening call experience already exists in the build — I implemented all five states plus the early-ended variant across earlier turns (in `screen-screening-candidate.jsx`): `ScreeningCandidate` (welcome/consent → channel choice → ready check), `ScreeningInCall` (live call with orb, transcript, help/topics side panel, bottom control bar), and `ScreeningPostCall` (confirmation + early-ended). They all share the same candidate chrome, EN/AR toggle, and explicit "AI" framing this spec calls for.

It's reachable from the Screening Agent's **"Preview a call"** action. Want me to:
- wire a clearer launch point (e.g., a "Preview candidate experience" entry on the agent settings/library), or
- apply any specific refinements from this spec (it matches the current build closely)?

Otherwise the candidate journey is already complete and live.

## User

<pasted_text name="Pasted text (609 lines)">
Design the CANDIDATE SCREENING CALL EXPERIENCE for "Connect AI", an 
existing AI-powered HR recruitment platform. This is the candidate-
facing side of the AI screening call feature — what the candidate 
sees from invitation through call completion.

This is a CANDIDATE-FACING surface (no admin sidebar, no internal 
user). The candidate received an email and clicked the link. They are 
not logged into a Connect AI account.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
CANDIDATE-FACING CHROME (different from admin app)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
- No left sidebar, no admin top bar
- Top: company branding ("Connect AI" logo small, optionally co-branded 
  "for [Hiring Company]")
- Bottom: small footer with "Powered by Connect AI" + privacy + help links
- Visual language matches Connect AI palette but with more generous 
  spacing and calmer tone — this is the candidate's experience
- Light theme, off-white background (~#FAFAF7)
- White cards with soft shadows, slightly larger padding than admin views
- Primary purple #6B5BFF, teal accent #5EEAD4
- Render in English (with EN/AR toggle visible everywhere)

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
DESIGN PHILOSOPHY — ONE JOURNEY, MANY STATES
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
The old design split the candidate experience into 3 separate screens 
(Pre-Call, In-Call, Post-Call). That made each screen feel disconnected.

The new design treats it as ONE journey with multiple states. The 
candidate moves through:

  1. WELCOME → consent → channel choice → ready check  (pre-call)
  2. LIVE CALL                                          (in-call)
  3. CONFIRMATION → next steps                          (post-call)

Each state has its own UI, but they share the same chrome, same tone, 
same visual language — so the candidate never feels like they've been 
handed off to a different system.

Principles:
1. Always tell the candidate what's happening and what's next
2. Make AI involvement EXPLICIT — never hide that they're talking to AI
3. Consent is prominent, not buried
4. The candidate chooses how to take the call — phone or browser
5. Trust through transparency, not stealth

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WHAT TO BUILD
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
A single React artifact with five states the user can navigate through 
(use useState for state management):

State 1: WELCOME &amp; CONSENT
State 2: CHANNEL CHOICE (phone vs browser)
State 3: READY CHECK (mic test for browser; phone confirmation for phone)
State 4: IN-CALL (browser path; phone has no UI)
State 5: POST-CALL CONFIRMATION

Render State 1 as default. Include navigation buttons to transition 
between states so the user can preview each.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SHARED CHROME (visible in all states)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar (60px tall, light):
  Left: "Connect AI" logo (~32px, small)
  Center: empty (or a step indicator in States 2-3)
  Right: 
    - Language toggle: [EN ●] [العربية]
    - Help link (small, gray)

Footer (60px tall, low emphasis):
  Centered text: "Powered by Connect AI · Privacy · Help"

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

STATE 1 — WELCOME &amp; CONSENT

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Main content (centered, max-width 720px):

  Heading (32px, weight 500):
    "Hi Ahmed, your screening call awaits."
  
  Sub-heading (14px, gray):
    "We're excited to talk with you about the Senior Frontend Engineer 
    role at Connect AI."

  ──── Hero card (white, generous padding, teal-accent left border) ────
  
  Top label (small caps, teal, with sparkle icon): 
    "✦ AI-CONDUCTED CALL"
  
  Heading (20px, weight 500):
    "This is an AI screening call"
  
  Body (14px, line-height 1.6):
    "Your initial screen for this role will be conducted by Connect 
    AI's AI agent — not a human recruiter. This is shorter than a 
    traditional phone screen and more flexible: you can take it 
    whenever you're ready, in English or Arabic, on your phone or in 
    your browser.
    
    Your conversation will be recorded, transcribed, and reviewed by 
    our recruiting team. The team makes all hiring decisions — the AI 
    doesn't decide anything alone."
  
  Three small info chips in a row at the bottom of the card:
    [⏱ About 15 minutes]
    [🌐 English or Arabic]
    [📱 Phone or browser]

  ──── Card "What we'll cover" (white) ────
  
  Header: "What we'll talk about"
  
  Compact list (no card per item, just bulleted):
    • Your background and work authorization
    • Your experience with React and TypeScript
    • Your leadership and team experience
    • Your interest in this role
    • Any questions you have for us

  ──── Card "Your consent" (white, teal-accent left border, prominent) ────
  
  Header: "Your consent"
  Sub-header: "Required before starting."
  
  Three checkboxes, each required:
    
    ☐ "I understand this call will be conducted by AI"
    ☐ "I consent to the call being recorded and transcribed for 
       evaluation"
    ☐ "I understand my recording will be stored for 90 days and 
       reviewed by Connect AI's recruiting team"
  
  Below the checkboxes (low emphasis):
    Helper text 1: "Prefer to talk with a human recruiter instead? 
    [Request human screening →]" (small link)
    
    Helper text 2: "Need to challenge the AI's evaluation later? 
    You'll have that option afterwards."

  ──── Bottom action area ────
  
  Primary button: "Choose how to take the call →" 
    (purple, large, full-width on mobile, disabled until all 3 consent 
    boxes checked)
  
  Below: small gray text "Can't take it now? Resume later from your 
  invitation email."

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

STATE 2 — CHANNEL CHOICE

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar adds a step indicator:
  "Step 1 of 2: How would you like to take the call?"

Main content (centered, max-width 720px):

  Heading (24px, weight 500):
    "How would you like to take the call?"
  
  Sub-heading (14px, gray):
    "Both options work equally well. Pick whichever is more comfortable."

  ──── Two large choice cards side by side ────

  Card A — "Phone call" (selectable):
    Card container: white, 12px rounded, click-to-select
    
    Top: large phone icon (lucide ti-phone, ~48px, gray)
    
    Title: "We'll call your phone" (16px, weight 500)
    
    Description (12px, gray):
      "Our AI will call you at your phone number. No app needed — just 
      answer when it rings."
    
    Below description, three small benefits:
      ✓ Works on any phone (smartphone or basic)
      ✓ Use your existing phone signal
      ✓ Can take it anywhere
    
    Selection indicator: radio circle at top-right corner
    
    When selected (radio filled, purple ring around card), expand below:
      Phone number input (pre-filled): "+966 50 123 4567"
      Country code dropdown
      Helper: "We'll call from this number: +966 11 XXX XXXX. Save it 
      as 'Connect AI' so you don't miss the call."

  Card B — "Browser call" (selectable, pre-selected by default):
    
    Top: headset icon (lucide ti-headphones, ~48px, teal)
    
    Title: "Take it in your browser"
    
    Description:
      "Talk through your computer or phone's microphone, right here in 
      your browser."
    
    Benefits:
      ✓ Works on any device with a microphone
      ✓ No phone signal needed — uses internet
      ✓ See live captions during the call
    
    Selection indicator: radio circle (filled by default)
    
    When selected, expand:
      Helper: "We'll test your microphone and connection on the next 
      screen."
      Sub-helper (small, gray): "Recommended: a quiet room and 
      headphones for the best experience."

  ──── Bottom action area ────
  
  Two-button row:
    Left: "← Back" (ghost link)
    Right: "Continue →" (primary purple, disabled until a channel selected)

STATE 3 — READY CHECK (browser path; phone path described below)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar step indicator:
  "Step 2 of 2: Get ready"

──── BROWSER PATH (render this as the default) ────

Main content (centered, max-width 720px):

  Heading (24px, weight 500):
    "Let's make sure everything's set up"
  
  Sub-heading (14px, gray):
    "A quick mic test before we begin."

  ──── Card "Microphone check" (white, generous padding) ────
  
  Centered visual: 
    Large microphone icon (~80px) with an animated waveform mock 
    around it (4-6 vertical bars with random heights, pulsing).
    Below the icon: status text in green
    "✓ Microphone working — say something to test"
    
    Alternative states (describe; don't render):
      If mic blocked: red icon + "Microphone access needed — click to enable"
      If no input detected: amber icon + "We can't hear you — try speaking"
  
  Below the visual, a compact tips card:
    Header: "Tips for the best call"
    Compact bullets:
      • Find a quiet space with minimal background noise
      • Use headphones if you have them
      • Speak clearly and at a normal pace
      • You can ask the AI to repeat anything

  ──── Card "Choose your language" (white) ────
  
  Two large segmented buttons (side by side):
    [English ●] [العربية]
  
  Helper text: "You can switch mid-call by saying 'switch to English' 
  or 'switch to Arabic'."

  ──── Card "What to expect" (white, compact) ────
  
  Header: "What happens next"
  
  Compact list:
    • The AI will introduce itself and confirm you're ready
    • You'll have a natural conversation — feel free to ask questions
    • Call lasts about 15 minutes (max 25)
    • Say "give me a second" if you need a moment to think
    • The AI handles silence — take your time

  ──── Bottom action area ────
  
  Big primary button: "I'm ready — start the call" 
    (purple, large, with phone-pickup icon)
  
  Below: ghost link "Save and continue later"

──── PHONE PATH (alternate; describe briefly, don't render as main) ────

If candidate chose phone in State 2, State 3 instead shows:

  Heading: "Confirm your phone number"
  
  Card "Your phone number":
    Display the candidate's number: "+966 50 123 4567"
    "Change number" small link
  
  Card "When should we call?":
    Three radio buttons:
      ● Call me now
      ○ Call me in 5 minutes
      ○ Call me in 15 minutes
  
  Card "Language" (same as browser path):
    [English ●] [العربية]
  
  Card "What to expect":
    Same as browser path, but adapted: "Your phone will ring at 
    +966 50 123 4567 in about 30 seconds. Save the number +966 11 XXX 
    XXXX as 'Connect AI'."
  
  Big primary button: "Confirm and wait for the call"
  
  After confirmation: "✓ Calling you now... Your phone will ring 
  shortly."

STATE 4 — IN-CALL (browser path; phone has no UI)

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Top bar changes (minimal, focused):
  Left: "Connect AI" logo (small)
  Center: Call status: "● Live · 6:23 / ~15:00" (pulsing green dot)
  Right: Language indicator: "EN ▾" (clickable to switch)

Main call area (centered, max-width 760px):

  ──── AI presence visualization (top) ────
  
  Large circular element (~140px diameter):
    A gradient orb or breathing pulse animation (purple/teal gradient, 
    soft, never harsh)
    Represents the AI's "presence" during the conversation
  
  Below the orb (centered):
    Small label: "Connect AI Assistant"
    Small teal pill: "AI Screening Agent"
  
  Status text (gray, italic, small):
    Currently: "✓ Listening — take your time"
    
    Alternative states (describe):
      "Speaking..." (orb pulses with rhythm)
      "Thinking..." (orb shows three small animated dots)
      "Paused" (orb is calm, gray)

  ──── Live transcript / captions card (the main focus of the screen) ────
  
  White card, comfortable padding, max-width 660px.
  
  Style:
    - AI messages: left-aligned, light gray text, small teal sparkle 
      icon prefix
    - Candidate messages: right-aligned, slightly darker text
    - Current speaker's message has a thin animated cursor at the end
  
  Sample (last 4 exchanges):
  
    ✦ AI · 5:42
    "Got it — six years of React experience, with the last three at 
    Acme Fintech. Can you walk me through a particularly complex 
    component you built there?"
    
    Ahmed · 5:54
    "Sure. We had a transaction timeline that showed up to ten thousand 
    transactions per user. The challenge was performance — we were 
    re-rendering the entire list on every state change."
    
    ✦ AI · 6:18
    "Interesting. How did you approach that?"
    
    Ahmed · 6:23 (current, with animated cursor)
    "We used virtualization with react-window, combined with memoization 
    on the row components. We also restructured the state so that filter 
    changes only..."
  
  Scroll-up indicator at top of card: "↑ Show earlier in conversation"

  ──── Side panel / contextual help (right of transcript, narrow ~200px) ────
  
  Sticky white card with three small sub-cards:
  
  Sub-card 1 — "Need help?":
    Compact action buttons:
      [🔁 Ask AI to repeat]
      [⏸ Pause for a moment]
      [🔇 Mute briefly]
      [💬 Ask for clarification]
    
    Small text below: "You can also just say these aloud — 'can you 
    repeat that?' or 'give me a second'."
  
  Sub-card 2 — "Today's screening":
    Progress checklist (small):
      ✓ Background &amp; work authorization
      ✓ React experience (in progress)
      ○ Leadership experience
      ○ Fintech interest
      ○ Your questions for us
    
    Small note at bottom: "About 40% through."

  ──── Bottom control bar (sticky bottom, full width, white card) ────
  
  Left side:
    Microphone state: large mic icon + "Mic on" (green text)
    Click to toggle mute. When muted: red icon + "Muted — AI is waiting"
  
  Center: (intentionally minimal)
    Small toggle: "CC: Captions on" (clickable to hide/show transcript)
  
  Right side:
    Small ghost icon button: settings (gear)
    Red button: "End call" (light red bg, requires confirmation on click)

  ──── Special in-call states (describe; don't render as main) ────
  
  Connection lost overlay:
    Full-screen amber banner:
    "Connection lost — reconnecting..."
    Timer pauses, transcript saved.
    When reconnected: "Reconnected. Picking up where we left off..."
  
  End-of-call transition:
    Status changes to "Wrapping up..."
    AI gives closing summary in transcript
    Smooth transition to State 5
